Aldi Just Dropped Everything You Need to Make Sourdough Like Taylor Swift
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/aldi-sourdough-kit/
Hayley Schueneman
Wed, 17 Sep 2025 21:35:34 +0000
Grocery Stores
New Products
News
Trends
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2183811
<p>It's a loaf story, baby, just say bread.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/aldi-sourdough-kit/">Aldi Just Dropped Everything You Need to Make Sourdough Like Taylor Swift</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>It&rsquo;s been a very busy year for Taylor Swift. She&rsquo;s fresh off of her record-breaking Eras Tour, she just regained ownership of all of her master recordings, and she recently <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/taylor-swift-travis-kelce-engagement-party-menu/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/taylor-swift-travis-kelce-engagement-party-menu/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">got engaged to Travis Kelce</a>. If this was a movie, well, the credits would be playing right now.</p><p>But if I&rsquo;ve learned anything from following Taylor Swift, it&rsquo;s that she never stops creating. In fact, her twelfth studio album, <em>The Life of a Showgirl</em>, drops in just two weeks. The studio isn&rsquo;t the only place where she gets in the creative mood though. On a recent episode of the <em>New Heights</em> podcast, Taylor revealed some of her favorite hobbies. Or, as she put it, &ldquo;I&rsquo;d say all my hobbies could be categorized as, like, hobbies you could have had in the 1700s.&rdquo;</p><p>We know <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-chai-cookies/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-chai-cookies/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Taylor likes baking cookies</a>, and it turns out that another of those hobbies is making sourdough bread. I need to know who feeds her starter when she&rsquo;s on tour! Details aside, I&rsquo;ve been trying to get motivated to get back into sourdough. The stars seem to have aligned, because Aldi just dropped a sourdough kit that has everything you need. Or should I say, <em>knead</em>.</p><h2>What&rsquo;s in Aldi&rsquo;s sourdough kit?</h2><p><img decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2183885" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Aldi-Just-Dropped-Everything-You-Need-to-Make-Sourdough-Like-Taylor-Swift_Courtesy-Aldi.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Aldi Just Dropped Everything You Need To Make Sourdough Like Taylor Swift Courtesy Aldi" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Courtesy Aldi"></p><p>Making sourdough bread requires a few advanced techniques and special tools. Think of this Aldi sourdough kit as having everything but the sourdough starter. It includes:</p><ul><li><strong>Bench scraper:</strong> You&rsquo;ll need this to divide the dough and to shape the dough into a loaf while creating surface tension.</li><li><strong>Dough whisk:</strong> Different from <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/whisk-types-guide/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/whisk-types-guide/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">French whisks and flat whisks</a>, a dough whisk is made specifically for thicker batters and doughs.</li><li><strong>Lame with two blades:</strong> Bread lames are one of the <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/bread-baking-essentials/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/bread-baking-essentials/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">essential bread baking tools</a>. Use these to <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/bread-scoring/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/bread-scoring/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">score your loaves</a> with all sorts of designs (besides aesthetics, scoring bread lets steam escape for a more even bake).</li><li><strong>Proofing basket:</strong> Also called a banneton, this is a lined basket that helps keep the shape of your loaf while it proofs.</li></ul><p>The best part is that you get all of these materials for $14.99. It&rsquo;s an incredible value, especially since you can use these tools over and over again to make plenty of loaves.</p><h2>When is Aldi&rsquo;s sourdough kit available?</h2><p>This kit is available right now at Aldi stores nationwide, while supplies last. Since it&rsquo;s an Aldi Find, it lives by the store&rsquo;s &ldquo;here today, gone tomorrow&rdquo; credo. That means that once they&rsquo;re sold out, they&rsquo;re gone for good. So if you&rsquo;re ready to enter your sourdough era, then it&rsquo;s time to take a &ldquo;Getaway Car&rdquo; to Aldi!</p><h2>Related:</h2><ul><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-favorite-candy/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-favorite-candy/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">I Tried Taylor Swift&rsquo;s Favorite Candy, and Now It&rsquo;s My Favorite Candy Too</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-pop-tarts-recipe/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/taylor-swift-pop-tarts-recipe/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">I Made Taylor Swift&rsquo;s Viral Homemade Pop-Tarts&mdash;Here&rsquo;s What I Thought</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/taylor-swift-super-bowl-party?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/taylor-swift-super-bowl-party?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">11 Ideas for a Super Bowl Party (Taylor&rsquo;s Version)</a></li></ul><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/aldi-sourdough-kit/">Aldi Just Dropped Everything You Need to Make Sourdough Like Taylor Swift</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
7-Layer Salad
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/layered-lettuce-salad/
Sharon Lehman, RDN

This colorful 7-layer salad is as beautiful as it is delicious. Build it in a clear glass bowl to show off the layers at potlucks, picnics and holiday celebrations.
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>1 medium head iceberg lettuce, torn</li><li>1 cup finely chopped fresh parsley</li><li>4 hard-boiled large eggs, sliced</li><li>2 large tomatoes, chopped</li><li>1 package (10 ounces) frozen peas, thawed</li><li>6 bacon strips, cooked and crumbled</li><li>1 cup shredded cheddar cheese</li><li>1 small red onion, finely chopped</li><li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>DRESSING:</b></li><li>1-1/2 cups mayonnaise</li><li>1/2 cup sour cream</li><li>1 tablespoon snipped fresh dill or 1 teaspoon dill weed</li><li>3/4 teaspoon dried basil</li><li>1/2 teaspoon salt</li><li>1/8 teaspoon pepper</li><li>Additional fresh dill</li>		</ul>

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>In a large salad bowl, layer the first eight ingredients. In a small bowl, mix mayonnaise, sour cream, snipped dill, basil, salt and pepper; carefully spread over salad.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Refrigerate, covered, several hours or overnight. If desired, top with additional dill.</span></li></ol></div>
Costco Wine Recall: Bottles of Prosecco Are at Risk of Shattering
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-wine-recall-september-2025/
Hayley Schueneman
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 22:56:32 +0000
News
Recalls
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2183830
<p>Check your wine rack and your fridge.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-wine-recall-september-2025/">Costco Wine Recall: Bottles of Prosecco Are at Risk of Shattering</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p data-start="195" data-end="502">If you picked up a bottle of Kirkland Signature Prosecco Valdobbiadene at Costco earlier this year, then you&rsquo;ll want to double-check your stash. Costco has issued a recall for certain bottles due to a safety issue that could cause them to break unexpectedly&mdash;even if they&rsquo;re just sitting unopened on your wine rack. Here&rsquo;s what you need to know.</p><h2>What caused the recall?</h2><p>According to a <a href="https://cdn.bfldr.com/U447IH35/as/3q6998t8pfg5hhjpkcpgvbc/FinalKSProseccoValdoMemberLetter" data-name="cdn.bfldr.com/U447IH35/as/3q6998t8pfg5hhjpkcpgvbc/FinalKSProseccoValdoMemberLetter" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">notice sent to Costco members</a>, some bottles of the Prosecco may spontaneously shatter&mdash;even if they haven&rsquo;t been touched. That&rsquo;s a serious safety risk, as flying glass could cause injury. Costco and Ethica Wines (the product&rsquo;s importer) are urging members to check their bottles and handle them with care.</p><h2>What stores sold the wine?</h2><p data-start="1014" data-end="1222">This recall only affects Kirkland Signature Prosecco Valdobbiadene, which is a Costco-exclusive brand. If you purchased Prosecco from Costco in any of the following states, it could be part of the recall: Iowa, Illinois, Indiana, Kentucky, Michigan, Minnesota, Missouri, North Dakota, Nebraska, Ohio, South Dakota and Wisconsin.</p><h2>How do I know if I have a recalled wine?</h2><p>Here&rsquo;s what to look for:</p><p><strong>Kirkland Signature Prosecco Valdobbiadene</strong></p><ul><li>Item number on the label: 1879870</li><li>Purchase date: Between April 25, 2025 and August 26, 2025</li><li>Costco location you purchased from was in one of the states listed above</li></ul><p>If all of those match, your wine bottle is affected.</p><h2>What should I do next?</h2><p data-start="1834" data-end="2031">Do not try to open the bottle, and do not bring it back into the store. To safely dispose of it, wrap it in paper towels, put it in a plastic bag, and place it in the trash. Then, bring the recall notice (or just your receipt) to your local Costco for a full refund.</p><p data-start="1834" data-end="2031">If you have questions, you can contact Ethica Wines at customercare@ethicawines.com or by calling 786-810-7132 Monday through Friday between 8 a.m. and 6 p.m. EST.</p><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-wine-recall-september-2025/">Costco Wine Recall: Bottles of Prosecco Are at Risk of Shattering</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
This Is Margot Robbie’s Go-To Breakfast Order
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/margot-robbie-breakfast/
Hayley Schueneman
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 22:30:09 +0000
News
People in Food
Trends
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2155795
<p>She's a millennial through and through!</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/margot-robbie-breakfast/">This Is Margot Robbie&#8217;s Go-To Breakfast Order</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>Margot Robbie is without a doubt one of the biggest stars of the moment. I&rsquo;ve been a huge fan of her work since her role as Tonya Harding in <em>I, Tonya</em>. She and <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ryan-gosling-favorite-dessert/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ryan-gosling-favorite-dessert/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Ryan Gosling</a>&nbsp;were absolutely iconic together in <em>Barbie</em>. Soon, we&rsquo;ll see Margot as Catherine in the upcoming adaptation of <em>Wuthering Heights</em>. And just this week, the newest film in her portfolio, <em>A Big Bold Beautiful Journey</em>, premiered.</p><p>When she&rsquo;s not on set, she&rsquo;s most likely working on her alcohol brand, <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/margot-robbies-favorite-cocktail/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/margot-robbies-favorite-cocktail/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Papa Salt</a>. It&rsquo;s an Australian-based, award-winning gin company that she launched with her husband and friends.</p><p>I wondered what she eats to keep up her energy for such a busy calendar. And honestly, as a fellow millennial, I am not surprised!</p><h2>What does Margot Robbie eat for breakfast?</h2><p>It turns out that she has a very specific <a href="https://www.vogue.com/article/margot-robbie-barbie-summer-cover-2023-interview" data-name="www.vogue.com/article/margot-robbie-barbie-summer-cover-2023-interview" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">avocado toast order</a>. Rather than smashing a few pieces of avocado on toast and calling it a day, she turns hers into a veritable feast by adding grilled halloumi and Australian bacon (a leaner, less fatty cut than American-style bacon). I love the idea of dressing up a basic combo like avocado and bread with a protein!</p><p>And when she isn&rsquo;t ordering avocado toast, she is having porridge with blackberries and a smoothie. She <a href="https://www.purewow.com/food/margot-robbie-red-carpet-ready-smoothie-recipe" data-name="www.purewow.com/food/margot-robbie-red-carpet-ready-smoothie-recipe" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">has said in interviews</a> that she particularly likes green smoothies (like <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-made-the-green-smoothie-reese-witherspoon-drinks-every-day/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-made-the-green-smoothie-reese-witherspoon-drinks-every-day/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Reese Witherspoon</a>), and her favorite recipe includes kale, apple and banana. What I love most about Margot Robbie&rsquo;s go-to breakfast is that it&rsquo;s something relatable that I could whip up right now.</p><p>Oatmeal and porridge is certainly a popular celeb breakfast, considering that people like<a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/what-does-kate-middleton-eat-for-breakfast/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/what-does-kate-middleton-eat-for-breakfast/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links"> Kate Middleton</a>, <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-breakfast-2025/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-breakfast-2025/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Ina Garten</a> and <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/willie-nelson-breakfast/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/willie-nelson-breakfast/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Willie Nelson</a> all enjoy it in the morning!</p><h2>Related:</h2><ul><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/5-ingredient-easy-breakfast-ideas/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/5-ingredient-easy-breakfast-ideas/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">40 Easy Breakfast Ideas for Busy Mornings</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/udon-carbonara/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/udon-carbonara/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">I Tried The Viral Udon Carbonara Everyone Is Losing Their Mind Over</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/timothee-chalamet-breakfast/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" Tyler Smith’s French Onion Sliders
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/tyler-smith-french-onion-sliders/
Tyler Smith
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 22:28:49 +0000
Burgers
Creator
Dishes & Beverages
Recipes
Sandwiches & Wraps
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2183937
These French onion cheeseburger sliders are the ultimate bite-sized indulgence. Juicy beef patties are topped with caramelized onions and melted cheese, all tucked into soft slider buns for a savory, melty twist on a classic. Perfect for game day parties or anytime you’re craving big flavor in a small package. —Tyler Smith, Virginia Beach, Virginia
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>3/4 cup butter, divided</li><li>1 large sweet onion, thinly sliced</li><li>1 large red onion, thinly sliced</li><li>2 tablespoons Worcestershire sauce, divided</li><li>2 pounds ground sirloin</li><li>1 envelope onion soup mix</li><li>1 tablespoon salt</li><li>1/2 tablespoon pepper</li><li>1 package Hawaiian sweet rolls (24 count)</li><li>12 slices Swiss cheese</li><li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>GARLIC HORSERADISH AIOLI:</b></li><li>6 garlic cloves, roasted</li><li>1/2 cup mayonnaise</li><li>1/4 cup sour cream</li><li>1/2 medium lemon, juiced</li><li>2 tablespoons minced chives</li><li>1 tablespoon prepared horseradish</li><li>1 tablespoon Worcestershire sauce</li>		</ul>

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>Preheat oven to 400°. Heat 1/2 cup butter in a large skillet over medium heat. Add onions; cook 5-6 minutes or until starting to lightly brown. Reduce heat to medium-low. Cook 25 minutes, stirring every 5 minutes. Add 1 tablespoon Worcestershire sauce, and stir to combine. Continue cooking until onions are a deep brown color and very soft, 15-20 minutes longer.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Meanwhile, in a large bowl, combine beef, soup mix, remaining 1 tablespoon Worcestershire sauce, salt and pepper; mix lightly but thoroughly. On a foil-lined baking sheet, shape beef mixture into a rectangle slightly larger than the size of the Hawaiian rolls (about 9x13-in.). Bake until a thermometer reads 160°, 15-20 minutes. Set aside.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a medium bowl, mash garlic with a fork until smooth. Add remaining aioli ingredients until well combined. Refrigerate until ready to use.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Reduce oven temperature to 350°. Without separating rolls, cut rolls in half horizontally; arrange bottom halves onto a parchment-lined baking sheet. Layer bottom halves with beef, caramelized onions and Swiss cheese; replace top halves of rolls. Melt remaining 1/4 cup butter; brush over rolls.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Bake until cheese is melted and buns are browned, 10-15 minutes. Garnish with additional minced fresh chives, if desired; serve with prepared aioli.</span></li></ol></div>
Tam To’s One-Pot Tomato Salmon

Alex Bala
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 19:44:26 +0000

https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2183899
Buffalo chicken egg rolls are the perfect mashup of comfort food and party snack. They're golden on the outside and creamy and spicy on the inside, and the first thing to go at the party! —Alex Bala, Longmont, Colorado
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>2 rotisserie chicken breasts, shredded</li><li>2 teaspoons onion powder, divided</li><li>2 teaspoons garlic powder, divided</li><li>1 pinch kosher salt</li><li>5 tablespoons unsalted butter</li><li>1/4 cup diced sweet red pepper</li><li>1/4 cup diced green pepper</li><li>1/2 medium red onion, diced</li><li>2 tablespoons diced jalapeno peppers</li><li>1 teaspoon ground cumin</li><li>1 teaspoon chili powder</li><li>1 teaspoon smoked paprika</li><li>1 package (8 ounces) cream cheese, softened</li><li>1/4 cup hot sauce</li><li>12 egg roll wrappers</li><li>2 cups shredded mozzarella cheese</li><li>1/4 cup neutral oil, for brushing</li><li>Optional: Ranch or blue cheese dressing</li>		</ul>

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>

In a medium saucepan, melt butter over medium heat. Add peppers, onion and jalapenos. Cook until tender. https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2182268
These bite-sized pumpkin truffles look and taste like pumpkins, thanks to pumpkin butter and puree mixed into the white chocolate and graham cracker base.
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>4 ounces white baking chocolate, broken into pieces</li><li>3 ounces cream cheese, softened</li><li>1/3 cup canned pumpkin</li><li>2 tablespoons pumpkin butter</li><li>1/2 teaspoon pumpkin pie spice</li><li>1-1/2 cups graham cracker crumbs</li><li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>SUGAR COATING AND GARNISH:</b></li><li>2 tablespoons sugar</li><li>1/2 teaspoon pumpkin pie spice</li><li>Miniature semisweet chocolate chips, for garnish</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Pumpkin Truffles%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/pumpkin-truffles/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0A4 ounces white baking chocolate, broken into pieces%20%0A3 ounces cream cheese, softened%20%0A1/3 cup canned pumpkin%20%0A2 tablespoons pumpkin butter%20%0A1/2 teaspoon pumpkin pie spice%20%0A1-1/2 cups graham cracker crumbs%20%0ASUGAR COATING AND GARNISH:%20%0A2 tablespoons sugar%20%0A1/2 teaspoon pumpkin pie spice%20%0AMiniature semisweet chocolate chips, for garnish%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>Place white chocolate pieces in a microwave-safe bowl. Cook at 50% power for 90 seconds; stir. Microwave at 30-second intervals until melted, stirring between intervals. Set aside for 5 minutes to cool.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a large bowl, beat cream cheese and pumpkin puree until smooth. Stir in pumpkin butter, melted white chocolate and pumpkin pie spice. Add graham cracker crumbs; stir until well-combined and a thick dough forms. Cover and refrigerate until dough is firm, at least 2 hours or overnight.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
To make coating, in a small bowl, mix together sugar and pumpkin pie spice; set aside.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Scoop chilled dough into tablespoonfuls; roll into balls. Roll in the sugar-spice mixture until evenly coated. Roll a toothpick or blunt edge of a knife gently into the sides to make the pumpkin's ridges. Top each with a mini chocolate chip to make the stem.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Store in an airtight container in the refrigerator until ready to serve.</span></li></ol></div>

Directions	</h2>

I Tried the New Popeyes x Hot Ones Menu—Here’s How Spicy It Really Is
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-hot-ones-menu/
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-hot-ones-menu/#respond
Joseph Erbentraut
Tue, 16 Sep 2025 14:58:49 +0000
New Products
News
Restaurants
Trends
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2183556
<p>The fast-food chain's new collab lets you pretend you're a celebrity across the table from Sean Evans. </p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-hot-ones-menu/">I Tried the New Popeyes x Hot Ones Menu—Here&#8217;s How Spicy It Really Is</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>There is no pop culture phenomenon quite like Hot Ones. Ten years ago, the YouTube talk show launched, and host Sean Evans has been alarming celebrities with probing questions and burning-hot wings ever since. In that decade, the show has amassed a cult following of more than 15 million subscribers and endless merch and internet memes.</p><p>It was really only a matter of time before a fast-food chain linked up with Hot Ones, and that&rsquo;s exactly what <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-ghost-pepper-chicken-sandwich-review/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/popeyes-ghost-pepper-chicken-sandwich-review/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">Popeyes</a> has done with its new Popeyes x Hot Ones menu. The menu is now available for a limited time, and I bravely tried everything.</p><h2><strong>What&rsquo;s on the new Popeyes x Hot Ones menu?</strong></h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2183572" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Tried-the-New-Popeyes-x-Hot-Ones-Menu_popeyes-hot-ones-2_Joe-Erbentraut-for-taste-of-home.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Tried The New Popeyes X Hot Ones Menu Popeyes Hot Ones 2 Joe Erbentraut For Taste Of Home" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="JOE ERBENTRAUT FOR TASTE OF HOME"></p><p>The new menu has four items. As a nod to the hit YouTube series, the offerings are available in ascending order of spice level:</p><ul><li><strong>Sizzlin&rsquo; Sriracha Dippers:</strong> These Chicken Dippers are said to be mild. They are marinated in pickled garlic Sriracha and served with a Last Dab Ranch dip cup and a fiery Sriracha sachet.</li><li><strong>Smokin&rsquo; Rojo Sandwich:</strong> This is the chain&rsquo;s iconic <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/we-went-to-8-restaurants-to-find-the-best-fast-food-chicken-sandwich/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/we-went-to-8-restaurants-to-find-the-best-fast-food-chicken-sandwich/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">fried chicken sandwich</a> topped with a medium-spicy Hot Ones Los Calientes Rojo spread, complete with the chain&rsquo;s signature brioche bun and tangy pickle slices.</li><li><strong>Darin&rsquo; Dab Ghost Wings:</strong> Popeyes&rsquo; <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-chicken-wing-restaurants/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-chicken-wing-restaurants/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">classic chicken wings</a> (available either bone-in or boneless) are dusted with a &ldquo;very hot&rdquo; ghost pepper dry rub. The wings are served with a Last Dab Ranch dip cup.</li><li><strong>The Last Dab:</strong> Iconic to the Hot Ones brand, the Last Dab sauce sachet (different from the ranch cup) lets serious heat seekers add a final &ldquo;extremely hot&rdquo; dab to their wings.</li></ul><h2><strong>Is the Popeyes Hot Ones menu actually spicy?</strong></h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2183571" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Tried-the-New-Popeyes-x-Hot-Ones-Menu_popeyes-hot-ones-1_Joe-Erbentraut-for-taste-of-home.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Tried The New Popeyes X Hot Ones Menu Popeyes Hot Ones 1 Joe Erbentraut For Taste Of Home" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="JOE ERBENTRAUT FOR TASTE OF HOME"></p><p>Far too often in recent years, fast-food chains have launched limited-edition spicy menu items that fail to bring the heat. I&rsquo;m happy to report that this was not the case here.</p><p>To stay true to the Hot Ones ethos, I began my tasting of the Popeyes Hot Ones menu with the most mild item: the Sizzlin&rsquo; Sriracha Dippers. I did not receive Sriracha with my order, sadly, so I dipped the chicken instead into the Last Dab Ranch dip. This dip caught me off guard&mdash;it was tangy and creamy as any good ranch should be, but it packed a bounty of heat that lingered on my tongue. Still, as spicy as it was, it was not heat just for heat&rsquo;s sake&mdash;it kept bringing me back for more.</p><p>Next, I tried the Smokin&rsquo; Rojo Sandwich, which was a bit of a letdown. After experiencing the spicy ranch dip, the heat coming from the Los Calientes Rojo spread felt much more mild and was overwhelmingly smoky, a flavor profile I don&rsquo;t personally enjoy. Still, the chain&rsquo;s chicken sandwich is beloved for a reason, so I can&rsquo;t complain too much!</p><p>Then, it was time for the Darin&rsquo; Dab Ghost Wings. The heat on the wings themselves comes from the dry rub. Most of the dry rub on my order had been knocked off the breading and sank to the bottom of the box, so I found the wings to be surprisingly tolerable.</p><p>Finally, it was time for the ultimate test: The Last Dab sauce. I fully went for it, feeling brave after two &ldquo;rounds&rdquo; that were less spicy than I had expected. I chose the wing with the most visible dry rub and squirted a large dose of the dab sauce on top.</p><p>At first, I was underwhelmed&mdash;and then the heat crept up on me, and I wished that my mouth could exit my body for a couple of minutes while my eyes watered and my throat tickled. Indeed, The Last Dab lived up to its hype.</p><p>All things considered, I was impressed by the Popeyes x Hot Ones menu and grateful that nobody was asking me questions while a camera captured my every move. The Last Dab Ranch is one heck of a dip, and The Last Dab hot sauce is, indeed, not for the weak.</p><h2>Related:</h2><ul><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-tried-the-new-mcdonalds-gold-sauce-and-it-tastes-like-sweet-smoky-heaven/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-tried-the-new-mcdonalds-gold-sauce-and-it-tastes-like-sweet-smoky-heaven/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">I Tried the New McDonald&rsquo;s Gold Sauce and It Tastes Like Sweet, Smoky Heaven</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-easy-appetizer/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-easy-appetizer/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Ina Garten Just Shared Her Easiest Appetizer Recipe Ever</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-genius-gourmet-sparkling-protein-drink-review/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-genius-gourmet-sparkling-protein-drink-review/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">A New Protein Drink Has Entered the Market, and You&rsquo;ll Never Guess What It Is</a></li></ul><script async type="text/javascript" Menu—Here&#8217;s How Spicy It Really Is</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>

<p>Looking for bubbly on a budget? Our Test Kitchen sampled 20 different bottles to find the best cheap champagne for your celebrations.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/the-best-cheap-champagne/">Cheers to the Best Cheap Champagne (Under $20 a Pop!)</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>

That&rsquo;s precisely what you get when you <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-to-open-a-champagne-bottle-the-right-way/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-to-open-a-champagne-bottle-the-right-way/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">pop open</a> a bottle of&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fbuywinesonline.com%2Fproducts%2Fcupcake-vineyards-prosecco-750-ml" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fbuywinesonline.com%2Fproducts%2Fcupcake-vineyards-prosecco-750-ml" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Cupcake Prosecco</a>.</p><p>&ldquo;This one is light, bright and crisp,&rdquo; says <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/author/shannon-norris/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/author/shannon-norris/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Shannon Norris</a> in the Test Kitchen. Testers picked up notes of peach and melon in this bottle. Despite the name and the fruity subtleties, Cupcake Prosecco isn&rsquo;t overly sweet. Shannon explains that this bottle of bubbly walks a fine line between dry or sweet.</p><p>This bottle, which retails for about $10, is a great people-pleasing option to include at your <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/how-to-set-a-table-for-thanksgiving/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/how-to-set-a-table-for-thanksgiving/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">holiday table</a>.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 2"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Cook's champagne or a bottle of the pricey stuff, to be on the slightly dry side, reach for&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fcooks-california-champagne-brut%2Fp%2F1478750" like a special occasion. This pale California sparkling wine is packed with lots of large bubbles.</p><p>Shannon shares that a sip of this cheap champagne is &ldquo;light, crisp and full of bubbles.&rdquo; It has notes of tart green apple and lemon zest. &ldquo;This is one I&rsquo;d drink, serve and cook with in my kitchen,&rdquo; says Shannon.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Rondel-Brut-Cava_via-totalwine.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="Rondel Brut Cava Via Totalwine.com" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 3"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Rondel Brut Cava</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="$11.99 at Total Wine" data-module="affiliate price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fcava%2Fbrut%2Frondel-brut-cava%2Fp%2F60170750" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Total Wine" data-retailer-name="Total Wine" data-product-name="Rondel Brut Cava" data-product-price="11.99" data-product-category="Wine" data-product-retailer="Total Wine" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow"><span class="dollar-sign">$</span><span class="sales-price">11.99</span> at Total Wine</a></p></div></div></div><p>Next time you&rsquo;re craving bubbles, our Test Kitchen recommends trying Cava, particularly&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fcava%2Fbrut%2Frondel-brut-cava%2Fp%2F60170750" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fcava%2Fbrut%2Frondel-brut-cava%2Fp%2F60170750" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Rondel Brut Cava</a>. This Spanish sparkling wine isn&rsquo;t as popular as Champagne or Prosecco, but it&rsquo;s absolutely fizzy and fantastic.</p><p>In fact, the bubbles in this bottle are what really stood out to our Test Kitchen team. Rondel&rsquo;s Cava was full of various-sized bubbles and held onto this fizz for a long time after pouring&mdash;three hours! That&rsquo;s pretty impressive says our Test Kitchen&rsquo;s <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/author/catherine-ward/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/author/catherine-ward/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Catherine Ward</a>, a lover of all things champagne. And remember, if you can&rsquo;t finish the bottle, you can <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-long-does-champagne-last-after-opening/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-long-does-champagne-last-after-opening/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">store opened champagne</a> for up to three days.</p><p>Beyond these bubbles, this Cava is wonderfully dry with flavors of pear and apple. These features make it a great complement to fish dishes and a striking yet welcome contrast to rich dinners. Give it a try with your <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-to-give-a-thanksgiving-toast/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/how-to-give-a-thanksgiving-toast/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Thanksgiving toast</a>! Keep a bottle of <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-non-alcoholic-champagnes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-non-alcoholic-champagnes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">non-alcoholic champagne</a> on hand for guests that prefer their drinks NA.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/19-Crimes-Snoop-Cali-Gold-Sparkling-Wine_via-totalwine.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="19 Crimes Snoop Cali Gold Sparkling Wine" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 4"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">19 Crimes Snoop Cali Gold Sparkling Wine</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="$12.99 at Total Wine" data-module="affiliate price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2F19-crimes-cali-gold-sparking-by-snoop-dogg%2Fp%2F346655750" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Total Wine" data-retailer-name="Total Wine" data-product-name="19 Crimes Snoop Cali Gold Sparkling Wine" data-product-price="12.99" data-product-category="Wine" data-product-retailer="Total Wine" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow"><span class="dollar-sign">$</span><span class="sales-price">12.99</span> at Total Wine</a></p></div></div></div><p>Snoop Dogg may have been pouring Chandon in his 2004 hit &ldquo;Drop It Like It&rsquo;s Hot,&rdquo; but these days he&rsquo;s popping open bottles of his own&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2F19-crimes-cali-gold-sparking-by-snoop-dogg%2Fp%2F346655750" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2F19-crimes-cali-gold-sparking-by-snoop-dogg%2Fp%2F346655750" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">19 Crimes Snoop Cali Gold Sparkling Wine</a>.</p><p>This California-made sparkler is pale in color with the <em>slightest</em> hint of green and &ldquo;refreshingly sweet,&rdquo; according to Shannon. It has a bold flavor for a sparkling wine with notes of lemon, nectarines and green apple for a crisp finish.</p><p>Made with a blend of Muscat and Riesling grapes (among others), this sweetness is no surprise. But it&rsquo;s a welcome flavor to pair with one of Snoop&rsquo;s favorite hobbies: baking. He picked up plenty of pointers while hosting a cooking show with the inimitable Martha Stewart! Martha also has her own wine with 19 Crimes: <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fwhite-wine%2Fchardonnay%2F19-crimes-marthas-chardonnay%2Fp%2F244087750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fwhite-wine%2Fchardonnay%2F19-crimes-marthas-chardonnay%2Fp%2F244087750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Martha&rsquo;s Chard</a>.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Domaine-Ste.-Michelle-Brut_via-totalwine.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 5"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="$14.99 at Total Wine" data-module="affiliate price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fdomaine-ste-michelle-brut%2Fp%2F1487750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Total Wine" data-retailer-name="Total Wine" data-product-name="Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut" data-product-price="14.99" data-product-category="Wine" data-product-retailer="Total Wine" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow"><span class="dollar-sign">$</span><span class="sales-price">14.99</span> at Total Wine</a></p></div></div></div><p>If you prefer a dryer sparkling wine, our team suggests adding&nbsp;<a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fdomaine-ste-michelle-brut%2Fp%2F1487750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fsparkling-wine%2Fbrut%2Fdomaine-ste-michelle-brut%2Fp%2F1487750%3Fs%3D1904%26igrules%3Dtrue" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut</a> to your list of must-try cheap champagnes.</p><p>This wine is made in Washington&rsquo;s Columbia Valley, a climate very similar to Champagne, France. You&rsquo;ll often see this brut labeled as American-style champagne&mdash;and it tastes like one!</p><p>This well-balanced, semi-dry sparkling wine has tart, Granny Smith apple notes, whispers of citrus and a toasty finish. While a bottle of Domaine Ste. Michelle Brut will only cost you about $12, &ldquo;it still feels special,&rdquo; says Catherine.</p><!--nextpage--><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Chloe-Prosecco_via-totalwine.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="Chloe Prosecco" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 6"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Chloe Prosecco</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="$14.99 at Total Wine" data-module="affiliate price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fprosecco%2Fchloe-prosecco%2Fp%2F159898750" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Total Wine" data-retailer-name="Total Wine" data-product-name="Chloe Prosecco" data-product-price="14.99" data-product-category="Wine" data-product-retailer="Total Wine" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow"><span class="dollar-sign">$</span><span class="sales-price">14.99</span> at Total Wine</a></p></div></div></div><p>For a fizz that stays and a flavor you&rsquo;ll adore, our Test Kitchen suggests <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fprosecco%2Fchloe-prosecco%2Fp%2F159898750" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2Fwine%2Fchampagne-sparkling-wine%2Fprosecco%2Fchloe-prosecco%2Fp%2F159898750" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Chloe Prosecco</a>.</p><p>This affordable sparkling wine is full of bubbles of all sizes. The smaller ones linger to help keep that fizzy feeling even after you&rsquo;ve been holding your glass for a bit.</p><p>Though, with the tart, fruit-forward flavors of this Italian bubbly, our Test Kitchen doesn&rsquo;t anticipate you holding onto your <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/best-wine-glasses-according-to-experts/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/best-wine-glasses-according-to-experts/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">stemware</a> for very long. This Prosecco hits all the right notes with a bit of green apple and nice acidity. &ldquo;It&rsquo;s very clean and bright,&rdquo; explains Shannon.&nbsp; &ldquo;I&rsquo;d be happy to toast with this one,&rdquo; she says.</p><hr><video id="T0733MN" title="Test Kitchen Preferred" data-description="Check out this video about our Test Kitchen Preferred process" poster="http://content.jwplatform.com/v2/media/ALzZ8JJI/poster.jpg?width=720" data-portal-copyright="Taste of Home"><source src="http://content.jwplatform.com/videos/ALzZ8JJI-OOHHzDJg.mp4" type="video/mp4"></source></video><h2>We Sampled 20 Bottles Under $20</h2><p>For this test, our <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/meet-the-taste-of-home-test-kitchen-team/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/meet-the-taste-of-home-test-kitchen-team/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Test Kitchen team</a> (many of whom are serious bubbly fanatics) sampled a whopping 20 kinds of affordable champagne in a blind <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/test-kitchen/taste-tests/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/test-kitchen/taste-tests/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">taste test</a>. That&rsquo;s right&mdash;no peeking!</p><p>But a few words on this cheap champagne taste test. To start, sparkling wine can only be called <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/what-is-champagne/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/what-is-champagne/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Champagne</a> if it comes from the Champagne region of France. If the wine comes from another region&mdash;even if it&rsquo;s elsewhere in France&mdash;it&rsquo;ll be called by another name. This being said, champagne (with a lower case &lsquo;c&rsquo;) has become the shorthand phrase for sparkling wine.</p><p>So for this test, our team used this expanded definition of champagne. They popped open bottles of all kinds of bubbly like Prosecco (an Italian bubbly), Cava (a Spanish sparkler) and even American sparkling wines. Each brand our team selected was under $20 and was scored for fizz and flavor.</p><h2>FAQ</h2><h3>Where can I buy cheap champagne?</h3><p>You can find cheap champagne at most grocery stores that sell alcohol, but one of our favorite places to order from online is <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2F" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.totalwine.com%2F" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">TotalWine.com</a>.</p><h3>How much is a cheap bottle of champagne?</h3><p>Cheap bottles of champagne ring up for $5 to $20.</p><h3>Does cheap champagne go bad?</h3><p>Cheap champagne, like other champagnes, go bad eventually. If you open your champagne, you can keep it for no longer than three days in the fridge.</p><div class="listicle-card-image-wrapper"><p data-wp-editing="1"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="size-large wp-image-1783324 aligncenter" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Taste-of-Home-Test_Kitchen-Preferred-The-Best-Products-Chosen-by-Our-Experts.gif?fit=680%2C674" alt="Taste Of Home Test Kitchen Preferred The Best Products Chosen By Our Experts" width="700" height="694" data-image-analytics='{"licensorName":"not available","credits":"Taste of Home"}' data-recalc-dims="1" title="Taste Of Home Test Kitchen Preferred The Best Products Chosen By Our Experts" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Taste of Home"></p></div><h2>Why You Should Trust Us</h2><p>Our Test Kitchen is constantly trying out new food, kitchen gadgets and cleaning gear. We put every product through a thorough&nbsp;<a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/about-product-testing/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/about-product-testing/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">testing process</a>. Then our Test Kitchen team chooses the winners. Those best-tasting and top-performing products get our stamp of approval: to be called <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/test-kitchen-preferred/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/test-kitchen-preferred/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Test Kitchen-Preferred</a>.</p><p>If you want to fill your pantry and fridge with the best products, check out these other tests:</p><ul><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-rose/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-rose/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">The best ros&eacute;</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-light-beer-brands/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-light-beer-brands/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">The best light beer</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-margarita-mix/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-margarita-mix/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">The best margarita mix</a></li></ul><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/the-best-cheap-champagne/">Cheers to the Best Cheap Champagne (Under $20 a Pop!)</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>

I Made the Viral TikTok Pickled Avocados and Wanted to Put Them on Everything
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/pickled-avocados/
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/pickled-avocados/#respond
Amanda Blum
Mon, 15 Sep 2025 22:57:28 +0000
News
Trends
Viral Recipes
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2177113
<p>Pickled avocados are a brilliant snack that can make unripe avocado edible and keep it fresh for a week.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/pickled-avocados/">I Made the Viral TikTok Pickled Avocados and Wanted to Put Them on Everything</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>My friends have long joked that in the event of a zombie apocalypse, my wall of pickled vegetables could sustain us for a few weeks of good eating. And despite having pickled my fair share of fruits&mdash;strawberries and cherry tomatoes being a couple favorites&mdash;I hadn&rsquo;t yet heard of pickled avocados.</p><p>Though there are plenty of <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/pickled-recipes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/pickled-recipes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">foods you can pickle</a>, avocados weren&rsquo;t on my radar until this summer, when videos of people raving about them took over my TikTok. Finally, a way to use up extremely unripe avocados instead of sitting around waiting for them to soften! Although the recipe for the <a href="https://www.instagram.com/reel/DJz39R4zHzw/?igsh=ZWVuOHF3cDE1cGJn" data-name="www.instagram.com/reel/DJz39R4zHzw/?igsh=ZWVuOHF3cDE1cGJn" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">viral TikTok version</a> was simple enough, I stuck to my own tried-and-true pickling brine recipe. The process is quick; it took less than 10 minutes to make two jars of avocado pickles.</p><h2>How ripe should the avocados be?</h2><p>Your best chance for success is to use very unripe avocados. Look for fruit with skin that is bright green. When you gently squeeze the avocado, there should be no give at all. I found more success with small to medium avocados, than with larger versions. Three small to medium avocados filled two pint jars (each jar fit one and a half avocados).</p><h2>How to Pickle Avocados</h2><h3>Ingredients</h3><ul><li>3 unripe avocados</li><li>1 cup apple cider vinegar</li><li>1 cup water</li><li>2 tablespoons salt</li><li>2 tablespoons honey</li><li>2 cloves garlic</li><li>2 tablespoons lemon juice</li><li>2 teaspoons coriander seeds</li><li>2 teaspoons mustard seeds</li><li>2 teaspoons peppercorns</li><li>1 jalapeno, optional</li></ul><h3>Directions</h3><h4>Step 1: Prep your jars</h4><p>Prepare two wide-mouth pint-size glass jars with lids. Plastic or metal lids are fine here. Thoroughly clean the jars. A dishwasher is best, but if you&rsquo;re hand-washing, rinse the containers with a bit of distilled white vinegar after washing, dump the vinegar and then, without rinsing, allow the container to dry.</p><h4>Step 2: Gather your ingredients</h4><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182257" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Made-the-Viral-TikTok-Pickled-Avocados_TOHD25_Pickle-Avocados_SarahTramonte_1.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Made The Viral Tiktok Pickled Avocados Tohd25 Pickle Avocados Sarahtramonte 1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Sarah Tramonte for Taste of Home"></p><p>Assemble your ingredients and divide the seasonings&mdash;the garlic, seeds and chili pepper&mdash;between the two jars.</p><p><em>Editor&rsquo;s Tip:</em> How much jalapeno you add is a very personal choice, but you should always use less than you think. Even a very small amount of jalapeno is going to make the pickles quite spicy. If you don&rsquo;t know where to start, cut a sliver of the pepper to place into each container.</p><h4>Step 3: Boil the brine</h4><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182256" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Made-the-Viral-TikTok-Pickled-Avocados_TOHD25_Pickle-Avocados_SarahTramonte_3.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Made The Viral Tiktok Pickled Avocados Tohd25 Pickle Avocados Sarahtramonte 3" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Sarah Tramonte for Taste of Home"></p><p>In a saucepan over medium-high heat, combine the vinegar, water, salt and honey. Bring the mixture to a boil and stir it until the salt and honey dissolve. Turn off the heat.</p><h4>Step 4: Cut and peel the avocado</h4><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182250" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Made-the-Viral-TikTok-Pickled-Avocados_TOHD25_Pickle-Avocados_SarahTramonte_2.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Made The Viral Tiktok Pickled Avocados Tohd25 Pickle Avocados Sarahtramonte 2" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Sarah Tramonte for Taste of Home"></p><p>Cut each avocado in half around the seed, and separate them. Using your knife, carefully remove the seed of the avocado. Since the fruit is unripe, you may find this harder than usual, but you can carefully lodge the knife in the seed and then carefully twist the knife so the seed pops out.</p><p>Using a vegetable peeler, peel each half of the avocado to remove all the skin. You should be left with pale green flesh. Lay each half, cut side down, on a cutting board and slice them the long way into wedges. Each avocado half should yield seven to eight wedges.</p><h4>Step 5: Place the avocados in the jars</h4><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182255" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Made-the-Viral-TikTok-Pickled-Avocados_TOHD25_Pickle-Avocados_SarahTramonte_4.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Made The Viral Tiktok Pickled Avocados Tohd25 Pickle Avocados Sarahtramonte 4" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Sarah Tramonte for Taste of Home"></p><p>Carefully place each wedge into the container, keeping them upright. Don&rsquo;t force pieces in; try to make space for them by turning the container on its side and tapping the side. Each container should fit one and a half avocados.</p><p>Add half of the lemon juice to each container, pouring it over the avocados.</p><h4>Step 6: Pour in the brine</h4><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182259" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Made-the-Viral-TikTok-Pickled-Avocados_TOHD25_Pickle-Avocados_SarahTramonte_5.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Made The Viral Tiktok Pickled Avocados Tohd25 Pickle Avocados Sarahtramonte 5" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Sarah Tramonte for Taste of Home"></p><p>Carefully pour the hot brine over the fruit, ensuring that all the fruit is completely submerged. You should have more than enough brine to fill two pint jars, stopping 1/2 inch short of the rim.</p><h4>Step 7: Refrigerate the pickled avocados</h4><p>Allow the containers to cool to room temperature on the counter, and then place them in the refrigerator. Wait at least 12 hours before trying your pickles.</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182261" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Made-the-Viral-TikTok-Pickled-Avocados_TOHD25_Pickle-Avocados_SarahTramonte_6.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Made The Viral Tiktok Pickled Avocados Tohd25 Pickle Avocados Sarahtramonte 6" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Sarah Tramonte for Taste of Home"></p><h2>How to Serve Pickled Avocado</h2><p>I mostly found myself eating the pickled avocado out of the jar with a fork. I kept returning to it, surprised by how addictive it was (much like any other pickle). While you probably won&rsquo;t want to cook with the avocado, it makes a fantastic garnish.</p><p>Layering segments on top of <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/top-10-grilled-fish-recipes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/top-10-grilled-fish-recipes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">grilled fish</a> or chicken was a wonderful way to use these pickles. The vinegar and brightness was a nice complement to the char of the grill. The pickles should have enough firmness to hold together if you chop them into a medium dice, which makes an even prettier garnish or addition to salsa. Since the avocados are preserved, they will retain their color and texture&mdash;even in the salsa.</p><p>Obviously, these pickles belong in tacos. You could replace your pickled onions with avocado pickles and get the best of both worlds: an acidic break from the taco filling, and the familiar taste and texture of avocado.</p><p>They&rsquo;re still avocados, and you can treat them as such by making a <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/easy-guacamole/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/easy-guacamole/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">guacamole</a> with them. It&rsquo;ll pack a different punch than traditional guac, with a satisfying vinegary bite.</p><h2>How long will pickled avocados last?</h2><p>These are <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/easy-refrigerator-pickles/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/easy-refrigerator-pickles/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">refrigerator pickles</a>, meaning that they haven&rsquo;t undergone a real canning process. Refrigerator pickles are best eaten within 7 to 10 days to ensure they stay nice and crisp. After that point, they may still be safe, but the fruit will begin to deteriorate and become soft.</p><p>The biggest threat to refrigerator pickles is the introduction of bacteria by using your hands to eat them, or reusing a fork that you eat off of. Only dip clean utensils into the pickle jar. If you see any white fuzz on the pickles, it&rsquo;s time to toss them.</p><script async type="text/javascript" src="//tracking.skyword.com/tracker.js?contentId=281474980448640"></script><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/pickled-avocados/">I Made the Viral TikTok Pickled Avocados and Wanted to Put Them on Everything</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/pickled-avocados/feed/

Elise Jesse’s Maple Dijon Salmon
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/elise-jesse-maple-dijon-salmon/
Elise Jesse
Mon, 15 Sep 2025 22:01:22 +0000
Creator
Dinner
Fish & Seafood
Ingredients
Meal Types
Recipes
Salmon
Salmon Fillet
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2183558
Looking for a quick, healthy, flavorful dinner with minimal cleanup? This maple Dijon salmon (or "pink steak" as my kids call it) with green beans is your perfect one-pan solution. Tender salmon fillets are topped with a sweet and tangy maple-Dijon glaze and baked alongside crisp-tender green beans, making for a delicious meal that requires less than 15
minutes of hands-on time. It’s my go-to for busy weeknights when I want something tasty, I don’t want to clean up a big mess, and I want to avoid the dinner plate struggle with the kids. —Elise Jesse, Cincinnati, Ohio
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>4 salmon fillets</li><li> Salt and pepper to taste</li><li>1 pound fresh green beans</li><li>Olive oil</li><li>1-1/2 cups water</li><li>1 cup uncooked basmati rice</li><li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>MAPLE DIJON GLAZE:</b></li><li>1/4 cup pure maple syrup</li><li>2 tablespoons Dijon mustard</li><li>2 tablespoons soy sauce</li><li>2 tablespoons olive oil</li><li>3 garlic cloves, minced</li><li>Coarsely ground pepper, to taste</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>Preheat oven to 425°. Season salmon with salt and pepper. Place salmon on one half of a parchment-lined rimmed baking sheet.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a large bowl, toss green beans with enough oil to coat the beans and salt and pepper, to taste. Place on the other side of the baking sheet.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Combine glaze ingredients in a small bowl. Brush over salmon filets. </span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Bake until salmon reaches an internal temperature of 145°, 12-15 minutes.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Meanwhile, rinse rice until water runs clear. Add to a small pot with 1-1/2 cups water. Add salt to taste. Over medium-high heat, bring to a boil. Reduce heat and simmer, covered, for 15 minutes. Remove lid, continue cooking 10 minutes. Fluff with a fork. Serve with salmon and beans.</span></li></ol></div>
20 Harry Potter Gifts for the Kitchen That’ll Make You Say “Accio”!
https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/harry-potter-inspired-kitchen-items/
https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/harry-potter-inspired-kitchen-items/#respond
Lisa A. Kaminski, Caroline Stanko
Mon, 15 Sep 2025 18:09:10 +0000
Stuff We Love
Stuff We Love Kitchen
http://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=collection&p=697771
<p>We've rounded up the best ways to bring some magic to your kitchen with these adorable (and practical!) Harry Potter kitchen gadgets.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/harry-potter-inspired-kitchen-items/">20 Harry Potter Gifts for the Kitchen That&#8217;ll Make You Say &#8220;Accio&#8221;!</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>

<p>The leaves are starting to fall, and the air is crisp and cool. You know what that means? A harvest-themed <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fcp%2Fthe-pioneer-woman%2F1231327" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fcp%2Fthe-pioneer-woman%2F1231327" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Pioneer Woman collection</a> is coming to Walmart!</p><p>Forget about springy florals and bright hues. This year&rsquo;s drop doesn&rsquo;t just contain familiar favorites. Instead, it boasts an assortment of new cookware and kitchen staples in seasonal shades. We also see the return of favorites like the coveted <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-ECI-DO-LINEN%2F16319416944" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-ECI-DO-LINEN%2F16319416944" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">pumpkin Dutch Oven</a>, which we consider an autumn staple.</p><p>No matter which piece catches your eye, we encourage you to snag your favorites soon. Many options are expected to sell out quickly.</p><h2>Our Favorite Fall Finds</h2><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Walmart-Just-Dropped_Pumpkin-Cast-Iron-Dutch-Oven_Via_walmart.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="Walmart Just Dropped Pumpkin Cast Iron Dutch Oven" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 2"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Pumpkin Cast-Iron Dutch Oven</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Shop on Walmart" data-module="affiliate no price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-ECI-DO-LINEN%2F16319416944" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Walmart" data-retailer-name="Walmart" data-product-name="Pumpkin Cast-Iron Dutch Oven" data-product-retailer="Walmart" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow">Shop on Walmart</a></p></div></div></div><p>A classic piece from prior Pioneer Woman fall collections, this <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-ECI-DO-LINEN%2F16319416944" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-ECI-DO-LINEN%2F16319416944" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">pumpkin cast-iron Dutch Oven</a> remains a seasonal staple. The 3.5-quart capacity, enameled cast iron construction and a whimsical gold stem knob bring a crisp weather flair to any gathering. It&rsquo;s oven safe up to 500 degrees Fahrenheit, making it the perfect pot for stews, braised beef and festive side dishes. This charming table centerpiece sells out every year, so we recommend snagging it in either orange or white before word gets out!</p><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Walmart-Just-Dropped_Pumpkin-Mini-Pumpkin-Cocottes_Via_walmart.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="Walmart Just Dropped Pumpkin Mini Pumpkin Cocottes" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 3"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Mini Pumpkin Cocottes</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Shop on Walmart" data-module="affiliate no price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-3PK-PUMP-COCOTTE%2F15940457810" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Walmart" data-retailer-name="Walmart" data-product-name="Mini Pumpkin Cocottes" data-product-retailer="Walmart" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow">Shop on Walmart</a></p></div></div></div><p>These <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-3PK-PUMP-COCOTTE%2F15940457810" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-3PK-PUMP-COCOTTE%2F15940457810" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">mini pumpkin cocottes</a> look cute as can be next to their larger Dutch oven cousin, but they&rsquo;re also versatile enough to justify all on their own. Each pumpkin in this set of three holds a half-quart&mdash;ideal for single-serving desserts, dips or side dishes. Unlike the larger version, each is dishwasher- and microwave-safe, making them the perfect pick for easy cleanup.</p><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Walmart-Just-Dropped_Pumpkin-Casserole-Baking-Dish-with-Wood-Lid_Via_walmart.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="Walmart Just Dropped Pumpkin Casserole Baking Dish With Wood Lid" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 4"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Casserole Baking Dish with Wood Lid</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Shop on Walmart" data-module="affiliate no price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FThe-Pioneer-Woman-Ceramic-9x13-Baker-with-Wood-Lid-Vintage-Lace%2F14735821554" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Walmart" data-retailer-name="Walmart" data-product-name="Casserole Baking Dish with Wood Lid" data-product-retailer="Walmart" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow">Shop on Walmart</a></p></div></div></div><p>Boasting a beautiful linen eyelet pattern, generous capacity and built-in handles, this <a href="https://go.skimresources.com/?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FThe-Pioneer-Woman-Ceramic-9x13-Baker-with-Wood-Lid-Vintage-Lace%2F14735821554" data-name="go.skimresources.com/?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FThe-Pioneer-Woman-Ceramic-9x13-Baker-with-Wood-Lid-Vintage-Lace%2F14735821554" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">casserole baking dish</a> is bound to delight at the next potluck. Use it for brownies or casseroles, and serve right from the dish. There&rsquo;s no need to transfer meals, since the dish itself is pretty enough for serving, thanks to the pretty lace embossing. In addition, the stylish wooden lid secures your famous dish inside, so it&rsquo;s easy to transport to parties while keeping the interior warm.</p><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Walmart-Just-Dropped_Pumpkin-Ruffled-Edge-Baking-Pie-Pan_Via_walmart.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="Walmart Just Dropped Pumpkin Ruffled Edge Baking Pie Pan" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 5"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Ruffled-Edge Baking Pie Pan</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Shop on Walmart" data-module="affiliate no price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-RUFF-BAKER%2F15673750496" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Walmart" data-retailer-name="Walmart" data-product-name="Ruffled-Edge Baking Pie Pan" data-product-retailer="Walmart" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow">Shop on Walmart</a></p></div></div></div><p>Have you ever seen a <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-RUFF-BAKER%2F15673750496" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPW-RUFF-BAKER%2F15673750496" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">pie plate</a> so pretty? The ruffled edge brings a touch of whimsy, while the durable stoneware construction ensures that tarts, pies and quiches bake evenly all over. It&rsquo;s also oven-safe up to 450 degrees Fahrenheit, so it&rsquo;s suitable for a number of delicious sweet and savory dishes.</p><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Walmart-Just-Dropped_Pumpkin-14-Piece-Cast-Aluminum-Cookware-Set_Via_walmart.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="Walmart Just Dropped Pumpkin 14 Piece Cast Aluminum Cookware Set" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 6"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">14-Piece Cast-Aluminum Cookware Set</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Shop on Walmart" data-module="affiliate no price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPioneer-Woman-14pc-Cookware-Set-Brown%2F14803571159" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Walmart" data-retailer-name="Walmart" data-product-name="14-Piece Cast-Aluminum Cookware Set" data-product-retailer="Walmart" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow">Shop on Walmart</a></p></div></div></div><p>Formerly available in turquoise, this <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPioneer-Woman-14pc-Cookware-Set-Brown%2F14803571159" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.walmart.com%2Fip%2FPioneer-Woman-14pc-Cookware-Set-Brown%2F14803571159" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">14-piece cast-aluminum cookware set</a> is now shoppable in both fall-inspired brown speckle and earthy charcoal.
