How to Shop at Costco for a Small Household
https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/costco-shopping-small-household/
Lesley Balla
Fri, 12 Sep 2025 14:00:14 +0000
Grocery Shopping
Home & Living
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=listicle&p=2180804
<p>Shopping at Costco doesn’t have to mean buying huge jars of mayo or a dozen boxes of cereal. Here’s how to shop for a small household.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/costco-shopping-small-household/">How to Shop at Costco for a Small Household</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<h2>Plan Your Meals and Go with a List</h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone wp-image-2181152 size-large" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Plan-your-meals-and-go-with-a-list_GettyImages-1288976536-e1757682430158.jpg?fit=680%2C454" alt="Woman checking her shopping list on her phone in a supermarket" width="700" height="467" data-image-analytics='{"licensorName":"not available","credits":"Goodboy Picture Company\/Getty Images"}' data-recalc-dims="1" title="Plan Your Meals And Go With A List Gettyimages 1288976536" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Goodboy Picture Company/Getty Images"></p><p>I&rsquo;m a big list-maker, and a list is particularly helpful when grocery shopping to keep me or my husband on track. Our running digital <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/expert-tips-for-a-well-organized-grocery-list/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/expert-tips-for-a-well-organized-grocery-list/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">grocery list</a> for Costco has go-to items and things we always keep stocked at the house. But the list also helps us think and plan for future meals. For instance, if we&rsquo;re entertaining guests, I might pick up extra organic greens for <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/salad-recipes-ready-in-30-minutes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/salad-recipes-ready-in-30-minutes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">salad recipes</a>, blocks of cheese for a <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/the-best-cheese-board-ideas-for-your-next-party/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/the-best-cheese-board-ideas-for-your-next-party/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">cheese board</a>, and meats to throw on the grill.</p><h2>Visit Once or Twice a Month</h2><p>The beauty of Costco is that you don&rsquo;t have to go every other day or even once a week. Buying larger quantities of items you can easily store for future use means going once or twice a month. We go <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/secret-grocery-shopping-tips/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/secret-grocery-shopping-tips/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">grocery shopping</a> at Costco about once every five to six weeks at my house to stock up on our usual suspects.</p><h2>Stock Up on Basics</h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2181153" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Stock-up-on-basics_GettyImages-2210920120.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="Shoppers At Costco" width="700" height="1024" data-image-analytics='{"licensorName":"not available","credits":"Robert Nickelsberg\/Getty Images"}' data-recalc-dims="1" title="Stock Up On Basics Gettyimages 2210920120" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Robert Nickelsberg/Getty Images"></p><p>It&rsquo;s not sexy, but <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-shopping-tips-will-save-tons-money/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-shopping-tips-will-save-tons-money/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">shopping at Costco</a> is essential for toilet paper, laundry detergent, toothpaste, pain relievers, dishwashing liquid, trash can liners and more. We have just enough storage space for the extras, so we never run out.</p><h2>Buy Things with a Longer Shelf Life</h2><p>Our pantry always contains dried pasta, olive oil and other cooking oils, crackers, coffee, <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/best-san-marzano-tomatoes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/best-san-marzano-tomatoes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">canned San Marzano tomatoes</a>, walnuts, oat milk and coconut water&mdash;all of which we buy at Costco. You can get many non-perishable items at the warehouse&mdash;including beer, wine and spirits, depending on your state.</p><h2>Shop the Frozen Section</h2><p>We always have three things in our freezer: organic frozen fruit for <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/healthy-smoothie-recipes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/healthy-smoothie-recipes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">smoothies</a>, organic broccoli for roasting or <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-stir-fry-recipes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-stir-fry-recipes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">stir-fry recipes</a>, and frozen, uncooked, shell-on shrimp for any <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/easy-shrimp-recipes-for-weeknight-dinners/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/easy-shrimp-recipes-for-weeknight-dinners/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">shrimp recipe</a> under the sun.</p><h2>But Don&rsquo;t Skip the Fresh Produce</h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2181154" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Dont-skip-the-fresh-produce_GettyImages-2198251468.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="Strawberries from Mexico are displayed for sale at a Costco Wholesale warehouse" width="700" height="1024" data-image-analytics='{"licensorName":"not available","credits":"PATRICK T. FALLON\/Getty Images"}' data-recalc-dims="1" title="Dont Skip The Fresh Produce Gettyimages 2198251468" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="PATRICK T. FALLON/Getty Images"></p><p>If your household eats a lot of fresh fruits and vegetables, Costco is a savior (especially during the winter months). We regularly stock up on fresh berries, greens or lettuces, mushrooms, carrots, sweet potatoes and baby potatoes&mdash;most of it is organic, too. I put Organic Girl power greens or organic spinach in just about everything, from <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/classic-pasta-recipes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/classic-pasta-recipes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">pasta recipes</a> to smoothies, so we&rsquo;ll always grab a box or bag.</p><h2>Premade Items Can Be a Lifesaver</h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2181155" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Premade-items-can-be-a-lifesaver_GettyImages-1572370439.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="Fully stocked Rotisserie Chicken display at Costco" width="700" height="1024" data-image-analytics='{"licensorName":"not available","credits":"UCG\/Getty Images"}' data-recalc-dims="1" title="Premade Items Can Be A Lifesaver Gettyimages 1572370439" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="UCG/Getty Images"></p><p>I&rsquo;ll never forget the first time I witnessed the Costco rotisserie chicken frenzy when they restocked the chickens. I avoided the scrum! But we&rsquo;ll occasionally buy a whole <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/best-grocery-store-rotisserie-chicken/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/best-grocery-store-rotisserie-chicken/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">rotisserie chicken</a> to divide up for several meals, from <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/chicken-salad-recipes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/chicken-salad-recipes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">chicken salad</a> to <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/simple-chicken-enchiladas/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/simple-chicken-enchiladas/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">chicken enchiladas</a>. Break it down and freeze the meat for later use, including the bones, which you can use to make <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/homemade-chicken-broth/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/homemade-chicken-broth/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">chicken broth</a>.</p><h2>Freeze Everything You Can</h2><p>We don&rsquo;t have a separate freezer (although sometimes I wish we did), yet we find room for freezing extra food in our run-of-the-mill kitchen freezer. We freeze meat, breads (the Costco ciabatta rolls are great for everything from burgers to sandwiches and croutons) and occasionally baked goods (muffins!). I love Tortilla Fresca Uncooked Flour Tortillas, which are found in the refrigerated section. They&rsquo;re raw and come in packs of two; we always freeze one.</p><p>We&rsquo;ll buy a pack of four New York strips, eat two and freeze the other two for another meal. Organic chicken breasts and ground beef are sold in smaller packs that are easily stored in the freezer. We&rsquo;ll freeze fresh crab meat if we&rsquo;re not going to eat it right away, and sometimes fish (depends on what it is and whether it was already frozen). And don&rsquo;t forget that you can <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/can-you-freeze-butter/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/can-you-freeze-butter/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">freeze butter</a>!</p><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/costco-shopping-small-household/">How to Shop at Costco for a Small Household</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
Pumpkin Spice Moscow Mule
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/pumpkin-spice-moscow-mule/
Susan Bronson
Thu, 11 Sep 2025 18:22:00 +0000
Beverages
Cocktail

https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2181296
The pumpkin spice Moscow mule is an autumnal twist on the classic, spiked with cinnamon simple syrup and real pumpkin.
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>1 cup sugar</li><li>1 cup water</li><li>4 cinnamon sticks (3 inches each)</li><li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>COCKTAIL:</b></li><li>Ice cubes</li><li>2 ounces vodka</li><li>1 ounce cinnamon simple syrup</li><li>1/2 ounce lime juice</li><li>1 tablespoon pumpkin butter</li><li>4 to 6 ounces ginger beer</li><li>Cinnamon stick, lime wheel, ground nutmeg, to garnish, optional</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Pumpkin Spice Moscow Mule%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/pumpkin-spice-moscow-mule/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0A1 cup sugar%20%0A1 cup water%20%0A4 cinnamon sticks (3 inches each)%20%0ACOCKTAIL:%20%0AIce cubes%20%0A2 ounces vodka%20%0A1 ounce cinnamon simple syrup%20%0A1/2 ounce lime juice%20%0A1 tablespoon pumpkin butter%20%0A4 to 6 ounces ginger beer%20%0ACinnamon stick, lime wheel, ground nutmeg, to garnish, optional%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>To make cinnamon simple syrup, combine sugar and water in a large saucepan. Bring to a boil; stir until sugar is dissolved, 3-4 minutes. Reduce to a simmer; add cinnamon sticks. Cover; simmer 5 minutes. Remove from the heat; let stand 2 hours. Discard cinnamon sticks. Transfer to an airtight container; chill until ready to use.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
To make the mule, fill a cocktail shaker 3/4 full with ice. Add vodka, 1 ounce cinnamon simple syrup, lime juice and pumpkin butter; shake vigorously to combine.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Fill a copper mug with ice. Strain mixture into the mug. Top with ginger beer. Garnish with a cinnamon stick, lime wheel and ground nutmeg, if desired.</span></li></ol></div>

<h2 class="recipe-nutrition-facts__heading">Nutrition Facts</h2>
<p>1 cocktail: 338 calories, 0 fat (0 saturated fat), 0 cholesterol, 37mg sodium, 54g carbohydrate (50g sugars, 0 fiber), 0 protein.</p>

The Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket Is Expensive, But It’s the Softest Throw You’ll Ever Touch
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/cozy-earth-cuddle-blanket/

Home & Living

https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2181149
<p>The Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket costs over $300. Our editor put this pricey blanket to the test to see if it's worth the hype.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/cozy-earth-cuddle-blanket/">The Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket Is Expensive, But It&#8217;s the Softest Throw You&#8217;ll Ever Touch</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>As a self-proclaimed blanket aficionado who has tested well over a dozen throws, I can confirm that even the <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-blankets/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-blankets/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">best blankets</a> are not &ldquo;one size fits all.&rdquo; For starters, there are the occasions. A movie night calls for a different cover-up than bundling up in bed with a case of the sniffles. Then, you have to factor in size, washability and weight. Heck, there are even <a href="https://www.rd.com/list/best-heated-blankets/" data-name="www.rd.com/list/best-heated-blankets/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener">heated blankets</a> and <a href="https://www.rd.com/list/cooling-blankets/" data-name="www.rd.com/list/cooling-blankets/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener">cooling blankets</a>!</p><p>Despite the overwhelming options, I&rsquo;ve found one blanket that is a game-changer&mdash;especially for gifting.&nbsp;Yes, it&rsquo;s pricey. But the <a href="https://go.skimresources.com/?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fcozyearth.com%2Fproducts%2Fcuddle-blanket%3Fvariant%3D42381575684276" data-name="go.skimresources.com/?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fcozyearth.com%2Fproducts%2Fcuddle-blanket%3Fvariant%3D42381575684276" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket</a> boasts the softest, snuggliest fabric I&rsquo;ve ever encountered. Here&rsquo;s everything you need to know about this gorgeous splurge option.</p><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" Amazon</a></p></div></div></div><h2>What is the Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket?</h2><p>The Cuddle Blanket is a faux fur throw made by luxury bedding brand <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fcozyearth.com%2F" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fcozyearth.com%2F" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Cozy Earth</a>. It features an ultra-soft, 100% polyester fabric that&rsquo;s incredibly warm and, well, cuddly. You can order the Cuddle Blanket in two sizes: standard (60&times;50 inches) and oversized (80&times;60 inches). It&rsquo;s currently available in three colors, as well as with &ldquo;bubble,&rdquo; &ldquo;double bubble&rdquo; and &ldquo;channel&rdquo; textures.</p><h2>How We Tested It</h2><p>I&rsquo;ve been testing the <a href="https://go.skimresources.com/?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fcozyearth.com%2Fproducts%2Fcuddle-blanket%3Fvariant%3D42381575684276" data-name="go.skimresources.com/?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fcozyearth.com%2Fproducts%2Fcuddle-blanket%3Fvariant%3D42381575684276" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">oversized Cuddle Blanket</a> in the dove grey colorway since June 2025.</p><h3>Packaging and Delivery</h3><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182172" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/The-Cozy-Earth-Cuddle-Blanket-Is-Expensive_Cozy-Earth-Cuddle-Blanket_02_Katie-Bandurski-for-TOH.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="The Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket Is Expensive Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket 02 Katie Bandurski For Toh" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski For Taste of Home"></p><p>The Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket arrived in a big brown box. Like other Cozy Earth bedding, it came tucked inside a really sturdy zip-top bag. This is one of my favorite luxe details about the brand, as I don&rsquo;t need to worry about tracking down a vessel for off-season storage.</p><p>I had read through the reviews explaining that the oversized blanket is heavy, and they were right! While not quite as hefty as one of the <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-weighted-blankets/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-weighted-blankets/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">best weighted blankets</a>, the Cuddle Blanket has more weight than your average throw. Keep that in mind if shopping for someone young, old or with limited mobility&mdash;it could be too heavy for them. The standard throw size and bubble styles are also a little lighter.</p><h3>First Impressions</h3><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182175" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/The-Cozy-Earth-Cuddle-Blanket-Is-Expensive_Cozy-Earth-Cuddle-Blanket_03_Katie-Bandurski-for-TOH.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="The Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket Is Expensive Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket 03 Katie Bandurski For Toh" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski For Taste of Home"></p><p>Right out of the bag, I was genuinely shocked by how soft the fabric was. I joked to my husband that it felt like chinchilla fur&mdash;or being enrobed in a giant <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/jellycat-food-plush/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/jellycat-food-plush/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Jellycat</a>. It&rsquo;s truly one of the softest things I&rsquo;ve ever touched.</p><p>Plus, on closer inspection, you can tell that it&rsquo;s a high-quality blanket that should last for years, if not a lifetime.&nbsp;There was also no weird chemical or packaging smells, which is always a plus.</p><h3>Daily Use</h3><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182176" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/The-Cozy-Earth-Cuddle-Blanket-Is-Expensive_Cozy-Earth-Cuddle-Blanket_04_Katie-Bandurski-for-TOH.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="The Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket Is Expensive Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket 04 Katie Bandurski For Toh" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski For Taste of Home"></p><p>Next, I got on with the most important tasks: lounging, snuggling and napping! I tossed the Cuddle Blanket on my couch and got right to work, err, rest.</p><p>As a born-and-bred Wisconsinite, I&rsquo;m familiar with the appeal of a good blanket. During a Polar Vortex, there are times when I would do anything to keep warm! The Cozy Earth blanket is oh-so-soft and weighted&mdash;somehow without being smothering. Yes, of course it is warm. But it&rsquo;s also still breathable.</p><p>For three months, I found myself reaching for the Cuddle Blanket at every chance. It&rsquo;s the ultimate companion for reading, watching TV or even working from home. I frequently found myself mindlessly petting the fabric while hanging out on the couch.</p><p>I noticed that the silky-smooth fabric does have a tendency to slip around. When napping, it&rsquo;s best to tuck a piece of the blanket underneath your body so it doesn&rsquo;t fall off. The size is also generous. While not quite as large as a <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/big-blanket-co-review/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/big-blanket-co-review/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Big Blanket</a>, the oversized throw is plenty large enough to share.</p><h3>Cleaning and Care</h3><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182183" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Cozy-Earth-Cuddle-Blanket-Is-Expensive_Cozy-Earth-Cuddle-Blanket_05_Katie-Bandurski-for-TOH.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket Is Expensive Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket 05 Katie Bandurski For Toh" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski For Taste of Home"></p><p>The one main con of the Cuddle Blanket? The oversized throw is, at least in my opinion, not safe for a standard home washing machine. Cozy Earth recommends machine-washing cold separately and hanging to dry; or for lasting quality, dry cleaning. I strongly suggest the latter.</p><p>My front-load washing machine has gone off balance while washing a queen-size duvet, and the Cuddle Blanket weighs twice as much. (And that&rsquo;s when it&rsquo;s dry!) It could potentially work inside an industrial-sized machine at a laundromat, but I&rsquo;m not risking a costly repair to my home washer.</p><p>Instead, I plan to treat the Cuddle Blanket similarly to an heirloom quilt. I&rsquo;ll spot-treat any spills and do my best to keep it clean. For this reason, it may not be the best option for households with a lot of everyday messes.</p><p>You can also consider opting for the smaller throw size. Editor Madi Koetting previously tested the standard Cuddle Blanket in 2023, and she ran it through the washing machine and laid it out to dry with zero issues.</p><h3>Pros</h3><ul><li>Over-the-top softness</li><li>Incredibly thick and luxurious</li><li>Weighted feel</li><li>Multiple color, size and style options</li><li>Comes in a giftable tote bag</li><li>Looks beautiful draped over a couch or chair</li><li>Makes an excellent gift</li><li>10-year warranty</li></ul><h3>Cons</h3><ul><li>Very expensive for a blanket</li><li>Oversized throw may not fit in a standard washing machine</li></ul><h2>What Other Reviewers Had to Say</h2><p>I&rsquo;m not the only one smitten with this out-of-this-world blanket. It&rsquo;s earned a solid 4.9-star rating on nearly 400 reviews.</p><p>&ldquo;Best blanket ever! I have no words as to how life-changing this giant, heavy, cuddly blanket is,&rdquo; says verified buyer Janice Y. &ldquo;Getting out of bed is harder these days. Even my dogs seem less anxious just from lying on top of it, and I find it funny that they slip and slide on the blanket. I mean, that is how soft it is! I&rsquo;m definitely gifting this to my friend who lost her house in the Palisades fires so she can have a sense of comfort and feel loved.&rdquo;</p><p>Another 5-star reviewer, Anh, echoes just how great a gift the Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket is: &ldquo;The Cuddle Blanket and Cuddle Pillows were Christmas gifts for my brother and his family. They absolutely love, love, love it. Soft, comforting, luxurious. The blanket came in a beautiful, large cotton zip-top tote that my sister in law was so excited to receive. The Cuddle Blanket is the perfect weight&mdash;this is a huge design achievement. It has no equal. You will love it and will be amazed at how comfy it is.&rdquo;</p><div class="oke-w-review-footer"><div class="oke-w-review-helpful"><p>Buyer ru c. recommends snagging this blanket when you see it on sale. &ldquo;I saw this blanket and was watching it for some time. It seemed so expensive, but the reviews were great, so I was able to get it 30% off and went for it. It is a dream! I think the first night I used it, I slept the best I had in a long time. It is warm and comforting if you are under it. Not sure how it does this, but if you lie on top of it, it cools you down. In menopause, I am always hot and cold, and this blanket is the best ever! Just got a second one. My whole family loves it! It also has that weighted blanket feel without being too heavy. Get one! I am serious! I just wish they made the matching cushion in burgundy, still, or I would get that too.&rdquo;</p><p>Any negative reviews revolve around the blanket not looking like the advertised color or being too heavy/slippery.</p></div></div><h2>Product Comparison: Cozy Earth vs. Lola Blankets</h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2171206" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/TOHA25_Lola-Blankets-Review_Mary-Henn_FT_OTedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Lola Blankets Review Mary Henn Ft Otedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="MARY HENN FOR TASTE OF HOME"></p><p>While there are dozens of <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-faux-fur-blankets/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-faux-fur-blankets/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">faux fur blankets</a> on the market, the Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket is most comparable to another luxury pick: <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/lola-blankets-review/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/lola-blankets-review/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Lola Blankets</a>. While both brands make a buttery-soft, oh-so snuggly throw, there are a few key differences:</p><ul><li>The Cuddle Blanket is only available in two sizes: standard (60&times;50 inches) and oversized (80&times;60 inches). Lola Blankets come in four sizes: baby (30&times;36 inches), medium (50&times;60 inches), large (60&times;72 inches) and The Lola XL (80&times;90 inches).</li><li>Prices are comparable, but the Cuddle Blanket is slightly more expensive. The standard Cozy Earth throw costs $278 while the same-sized medium Lola Blanket is $249. That said, Cozy Earth frequently runs sales of 20% off or more, which helps bring the price down.</li><li>Lola Blankets come in over three dozen colors and patterns, though many are sold out. The Cozy Earth blanket is currently only available in three hues.</li><li>Cozy Earth Cuddle Blankets come with a 100-night sleep trial and 10-year warranty. Lola Blankets have a 14-day return window and must be unused, unwashed and in the original packaging.</li></ul><h2>Final Verdict</h2><p>I came into this review with every hope of finding that there&rsquo;s <em>no way</em> a blanket is worth over $300. I&rsquo;m afraid I was proven wrong. The Cuddle Blanket is absolutely a splurge, but it does, in fact, live up to the hype. I have yet to encounter another comparable blanket on the market that is as uber-soft, cozy and high-quality. Plus, it makes an incredible holiday gift. Our team of editors has tested over a dozen products from the brand, including pajamas, sheets, comforters, blankets and towels. Across the board, we find Cozy Earth offers high-quality, luxurious products that elevate your day-to-day routine. Read more in our full <a href="https://www.rd.com/article/cozy-earth-review/" data-name="www.rd.com/article/cozy-earth-review/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Cozy Earth review</a>.</p><h3>Why is Cozy Earth so expensive?</h3><p>Cozy Earth sells luxury bedding, so its prices are often elevated above other products on the market. The brand is committed to fair labor practices and sustainability, plus it avoids harmful chemicals. Cozy Earth bedding also comes with a <a href="https://cozyearth.com/pages/warranty" data-name="cozyearth.com/pages/warranty" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">10-year warranty</a> that protects against defects.</p><h2>Why You Should Trust Us</h2><p>Here at&nbsp;<em>Taste of Home</em>, we&rsquo;re on a quest to discover the&nbsp;best blankets&nbsp;on the market. To date, we&rsquo;ve tested over 50 options across a variety of categories, including weighted and&nbsp;faux fur&nbsp;picks. We&rsquo;ve tried all the top brands, including Cozy Earth,&nbsp;Lola Blankets, Quince, Barefoot Dreams and more. Our editors have spent countless hours snuggling, napping and hosting movie nights. (Tough job, I know.)</p><p>Lead tester for this piece, Katie Bandurski, has nearly a decade of editorial experience. She&rsquo;s reviewed hundreds of products in the home and kitchen space, including&nbsp;<a tabindex="0" href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/weighted-stuffed-animals/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/weighted-stuffed-animals/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" aria-label="weighted stuffed animals">weighted stuffed animals</a>,&nbsp;<a href="https://www.rd.com/list/best-cooling-comforters/" data-name="www.rd.com/list/best-cooling-comforters/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener">cooling comforters</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a tabindex="0" href="https://www.rd.com/list/best-pajamas-for-women/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-name="www.rd.com/list/best-pajamas-for-women/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" aria-label="pajamas for women">pajamas for women</a>.</p><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/cozy-earth-cuddle-blanket/">The Cozy Earth Cuddle Blanket Is Expensive, But It&#8217;s the Softest Throw You&#8217;ll Ever Touch</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
Tumble Rugs Review: Do These Washable Rugs Really Live Up to the Hype?
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/tumble-rugs-review/
Katie Bandurski
Thu, 11 Sep 2025 15:31:53 +0000
Home & Living
Home Decor
Product Tests
Stuff We Love
Stuff We Love Home
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2180700
<p>We tested a Tumble rug for three months. Here's how it went.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/tumble-rugs-review/">Tumble Rugs Review: Do These Washable Rugs Really Live Up to the Hype?</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>I grew up in a house with white carpeting. When spills happened, it was an all-hands-on-deck approach to remove splotches of juice, spaghetti sauce or coffee from the fibers.</p><p>Now, as an adult with my own space, I&rsquo;m happy to skip the stress of spills by opting for washable rugs. These easy-to-clean floor coverings offer the same cushy benefits as rugs or carpeting but are able to handle life&rsquo;s ickiest messes.</p><p>After trying (and loving) <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ruggable-reviews/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ruggable-reviews/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Ruggable</a>, I put another popular washable rug brand to the test. Here&rsquo;s my honest <a href="https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fcollections%2Fall" data-name="www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fcollections%2Fall" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Tumble Rugs</a> review.</p><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Olivia_Ivory_Neutral-Livingroom_Via-tumbleliving.com_.jpg?w=680" alt="Olivia Ivory Neutral Livingroom" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 1"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h2 class="ap-card-superlative">We Tried It</h2><h3 class="ap-card-title">Tumble Rugs</h3></div><div class="ap-card-description"><p>Banish stains once and for all with a washable Tumble rug.</p></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Shop on Tumble" data-module="affiliate no price button" data-position="" href="https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fcollections%2Fall" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Tumble" data-retailer-name="Tumble" data-product-name="Tumble Rugs" data-product-retailer="Tumble" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow">Shop on Tumble</a></p></div></div></div><h2>What are Tumble Rugs?</h2><p>Tumble is a washable rug brand that specializes in life-proof floor decor. Each rug is spill-proof and meant to withstand messes from kids and pets. There are more than 80 Tumble rug styles to choose from, all designed by hand and illustrated in-house. Tumble rugs fit in a standard washing machine and are priced slightly below comparable washable rug brands, like Ruggable.</p><h2>How We Tested It</h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182107" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_01_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 01 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski for Taste of Home"></p><p>I&rsquo;ve been testing the <a href="https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fproducts%2Folivia-ivory-neutral" data-name="www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fproducts%2Folivia-ivory-neutral" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">8&times;10 Olivia ivory and neutral rug</a> since June 2025. In that time, it has lived in my husband&rsquo;s office, where it sees daily foot traffic.</p><h3>Packaging and Delivery</h3><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182108" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_02_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 02 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski for Taste of Home"></p><p>My Tumble rug arrived in a flat brown box. It included the rug topper, 12 rug pad sections and four rug corner grippers, along with some setup information. I was very intrigued by the rug pad; it reminded me of the rubber gym flooring you can puzzle-piece together.</p><p>The rug topper was soft and felt very durable. Some washable rugs can look like a piece of fabric thrown on the floor, but the Tumble has a beautiful texture and reinforced edges, which help it look like a standard rug. That said, it doesn&rsquo;t have a plush, cushy feel.</p><h3>Set-Up</h3><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182109" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_03_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 03 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski for Taste of Home"></p><p>Initially, I planned to put the Tumble rug in my media room under our <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-modular-sectionals/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-modular-sectionals/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">modular sectional</a>. Tumble recommends starting with a clear space since the rug pad is difficult to move once it&rsquo;s in place. Since the room is so small (and full of furniture!) I couldn&rsquo;t quite clear off an entire 8&times;10 section. Keep this in mind if you&rsquo;re looking to put a Tumble rug in a crowded room.</p><p>Instead, I moved the rug up to my husband&rsquo;s office, where there was plenty of floor space. I started laying out the floor pad&mdash;each piece is numbered and has a specific spot, just like a puzzle. You connect each piece by aligning the interlocking teeth and pushing down, again, just like a puzzle.</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182115" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_04_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 04 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Banndurski for Taste of Home"></p><p>This process is simple in theory, but it was surprisingly tedious and time-consuming. Any time I would connect a new piece, some of the others would loosen, and I&rsquo;d have to go back to reattach them. If I tried to re-center or straighten the pad, the same thing would happen. I even pulled too hard on one of the pieces, and one of the teeth fell off. (Oops!) Plus, it can be hard to tell exactly where you want the rug in your space until it&rsquo;s laid out, but this pad process makes the ensemble very difficult to move once you get started.</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182131" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_07_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 07 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski for Taste of Home"></p><p>After about 45 minutes of finagling, I finally got my pad exactly where I wanted it. Luckily, the rug topper is very easy to attach. Simply lay it on top and tuck each pad corner into the pockets on the rug&rsquo;s underside.&nbsp;I noticed some pretty severe wrinkles on my rug topper. The brand notes that you can use an iron on the lowest setting to smooth them out, if desired.</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182132" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_09_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 09 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski for Taste of Home"></p><p>Lastly, before you move any furniture back onto your rug, apply the corner grippers. These sticky, silicone pieces attach directly to the floor and keep the rug in place.</p><h3>Day-to-Day Wear</h3><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182139" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_06_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 06 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski for Taste of Home"></p><p>Once the rug was in place and the furniture arranged, it was time to step back and admire my handiwork. What a difference! My husband&rsquo;s office is in major need of a refresh. The walls are currently a bright orange and yellow (!!!), but the rug really helped bring the space together while we make plans to paint or wallpaper.</p><p>After a week or two of use, I noticed that the rolling chair he uses at his desk causes the rug to wrinkle and bunch a bit. This is likely because the rug only engages with the pad at the corners. It&rsquo;s not a huge deal, but it does require us to adjust the rug every few days to avoid a tripping hazard. The brand does note that this can happen and <a href="https://www.tumbleliving.com/pages/faqs?hcUrl=%2Fen-US%2Fcan-a-tumble-rug-be-used-underneath-rolling-furniture-or-chairs-116977" data-name="www.tumbleliving.com/pages/faqs?hcUrl=%2Fen-US%2Fcan-a-tumble-rug-be-used-underneath-rolling-furniture-or-chairs-116977" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">recommends avoiding the use of rolling chairs</a>, so keep that in mind if shopping for a home office.</p><p>That said, the Tumble rug has held up beautifully to the pressure of the chair&rsquo;s wheels. The previous rug we had in the office got matted and mangled after just a month or two, and you can&rsquo;t see any excessive signs of wear on the Tumble rug.</p><p>When walking on the rug, the pad does provide a really nice cushion. It reminds me of a thick yoga mat! We had overnight guests stay over on an air mattress, and it was a really nice upgrade from the cold, hardwood floor.</p><h3>Cleaning</h3><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182142" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_10_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 10 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski for Taste of Home"></p><p>Now, for the main event: Is a Tumble rug really washable? Yes! The <a href="https://www.tumbleliving.com/pages/faqs?hcUrl=%2Fen-US%2Fdo-all-tumble-rugs-fit-in-a-washing-machine-232581" data-name="www.tumbleliving.com/pages/faqs?hcUrl=%2Fen-US%2Fdo-all-tumble-rugs-fit-in-a-washing-machine-232581" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">brand advertises</a>&nbsp;that all of its rugs are designed to fit in a standard washer and dryer.&nbsp;So, after two months of use, I put this claim to the test.</p><p>First, I intentionally stained the rug with coffee and ketchup to see if these common spills would come out in the wash. Then, I removed it from the pad and stuffed it in my front-load washing machine, keeping the stained side facing out. I used a mild detergent and washed it on a cold, delicate cycle.</p><p>I was a little concerned that my machine would error due to an uneven load. (This has happened before when washing duvets or really heavy blankets.) But it managed just fine!</p><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182151" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_15_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 15 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski for Taste of Home"></p><p>To dry, I used low heat for 50 minutes. It was still pretty wet and kept bunching up, so I moved on to air drying. I hung the rug over the bar in my shower, and it took a day to fully dry. The good news? All stains lifted out in the wash&mdash;even without pre-treating.</p><p>While the washing test was a success, I will say that I have a lot of trouble vacuuming the Tumble rug. My Dyson V15 always wants to &ldquo;eat&rdquo; the rug, and since it&rsquo;s so loosely connected to the pad, it succeeds. When I have dry spills, like cereal or other crumbs, I need to resort to using a hand vacuum, which is tedious.</p><h3>Pros</h3><ul><li>Beautiful neutral design</li><li>Truly fits in a standard washing machine</li><li>Stains lift out easily</li><li>Rug pad adds a nice cushion underfoot</li><li>Corners are nonslip and help the rug lie flat</li><li>Fibers stand up to heavy wear and tear</li><li>Spills bead on the surface and are easy to wipe up</li></ul><h3>Cons</h3><ul><li>Pad system is very frustrating to put down</li><li>Rug tends to bunch, especially when vacuuming</li><li>Not as plush as a standard rug</li></ul><h2>What Other Reviewers Had to Say</h2><p>I&rsquo;m not the only one who was impressed by the Olivia Tumble Rug. It&rsquo;s earned a solid 4.8 stars from over 1,700 reviewers.</p><p>&ldquo;I am so excited I get to have a light and bright entry rug!&rdquo; says verified buyer Rachel C. &ldquo;Usually, I would pick something dark to cover stains and dirt until I got around to having it cleaned. (Goodbye money). It&rsquo;s SO awesome I can throw this in the wash when needed!&rdquo;</p><p>Four-star reviewer Kaenani F. was impressed with how the Tumble rug stands up to pet stains. &ldquo;Truly liquid repellent. My puppy peed on the carpet the day after I got it, and it sat for 30 minutes before I got home&hellip;It wiped right off with a paper towel! I sprayed it, and it was good to go. Only complaint is it&rsquo;s more gray than ivory and cream as pictured.&rdquo;</p><p>Negative reviews of the rug center around the color not being as neutral as pictured or shipping delays.</p><h2>Product Comparison: Tumble vs. Ruggable</h2><p>I&rsquo;ve tested both Tumble and Ruggable rugs in my home, and there are a few key differences:</p><ul><li>Tumble offers roughly 80 rug styles, whereas Ruggable has hundreds. If you want more choices, including designer collaborations, Ruggable is a better bet.</li><li>The Tumble pad uses interlocking pieces you lay out like a puzzle. This results in a cushy, comfy feel underfoot. But it also means the rug is less engaged with the pad, which can cause bunching. The pad is also difficult to move once it&rsquo;s laid out. Ruggable uses a hook-and-loop tape to firmly connect the rug pad with the cover. It&rsquo;s easy to move both pieces around, and they&rsquo;re fully connected. That said, unfurling the Ruggable cover onto the pad can be tricky with larger sizes.</li><li>Tumble rugs fit into most standard washing machines. Ruggable flat-woven rugs do, too. But, as detailed in my <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ruggable-rug/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ruggable-rug/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Ruggable 6&times;9 rug review</a>, there are exceptions for the thicker tufted styles.</li><li>Tumble sells rugs and kids&rsquo; play mats. Ruggable sells rugs, doormats, bath mats, pillows, pet beds and more.</li></ul><h2>Final Verdict</h2><p>While Tumble rugs have a few quirks, I found that they&rsquo;re a solid option for washable rugs. Yes, the pad can be tricky to place, but it&rsquo;s also very cushioned and provides support. It&rsquo;s not the most plush option, but it washes up like a dream, even after coffee and ketchup stains. Plus, they&rsquo;re built to last with high-quality fabrics and construction. After wear-testing in my home for over three months, I&rsquo;m confident this is a quality option that will stand up to years of daily life.</p><h2>Where to Buy</h2><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/Olivia_Ivory_Neutral-Livingroom_Via-tumbleliving.com_1.jpg?w=680" alt="Olivia Ivory Neutral Livingroom" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 11"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h2 class="ap-card-superlative">We Tried It</h2><h3 class="ap-card-title">Tumble Rugs</h3></div><div class="ap-card-description"><p>This washable rug is up for any task&mdash;from spills to pet messes.</p></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Shop on Tumble" data-module="affiliate no price button" data-position="" href="https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fcollections%2Fall" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop on Tumble" data-retailer-name="Tumble" data-product-name="Tumble Rugs" data-product-retailer="Tumble" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow">Shop on Tumble</a></p></div></div></div><p>You can pick up a Tumble rug directly on the <a href="https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fcollections%2Fall" data-name="www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fcollections%2Fall" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">brand&rsquo;s website</a>. Prices range depending on size and style, and the exact <a href="https://www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fproducts%2Folivia-ivory-neutral" data-name="www.awin1.com/cread.php?awinmid=104493&amp;awinaffid=622885&amp;ued=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tumbleliving.com%2Fproducts%2Folivia-ivory-neutral" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">8&times;10 Olivia ivory and neutral rug</a> I tested costs $439.</p><hr><h2>FAQ</h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182153" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/TOHA25_Tumble-Rugs_Katie-Bandurski_17_YVedit.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="Toha25 Tumble Rugs Katie Bandurski 17 Yvedit" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Katie Bandurski for Taste of Home"></p><h3>How do you wash a Tumble rug?</h3><p>To wash a Tumble rug, place it in your washing machine with any stains facing out. (You can also pre-treat any deep-set stains.) Wash on a cold, gentle cycle with mild detergent. Air-dry or use a low dryer setting.</p><h3>Are Tumble rugs good?</h3><p>Yes! We found that they offer impressive quality at a fair price. They also are just as easy to wash as advertised.</p><h3>Do Tumble rugs ever go on sale?</h3><p>Yes, the brand offers discounts throughout the year, typically aligned with major sales events like Amazon Prime Day and Labor Day.</p><h2>Why You Should Trust Us</h2><p>Here at&nbsp;<em>Taste of Home</em>, it is quite literally our job to evaluate home and kitchen products. And we take that responsibility seriously! We thoroughly vet products through fair, accurate testing methodologies. Our team has combined decades of experience in the home, kitchen and lifestyle spaces.</p><p>The tester for this Ruggable runner evaluation, Katie Bandurski, has nearly a decade of experience in the media industry covering food, kitchen, home and garden trends. She extensively covers home care, including other washable rugs, doormats and home furnishings.</p><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/tumble-rugs-review/">Tumble Rugs Review: Do These Washable Rugs Really Live Up to the Hype?</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
The Fans Have Spoken: Cracker Barrel Is Halting Plans to Remodel
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/cracker-barrel-halts-plans-to-remodel/
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/cracker-barrel-halts-plans-to-remodel/#respond
Melany Love
Thu, 11 Sep 2025 00:14:18 +0000
News
Restaurants
Trends
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2182584
<p>The Southern-themed restaurant will keep its current logo and discontinue plans for an interior redesign.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/cracker-barrel-halts-plans-to-remodel/">The Fans Have Spoken: Cracker Barrel Is Halting Plans to Remodel</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>If you&rsquo;re a foodie like me, there&rsquo;s no doubt you&rsquo;ve heard about Cracker Barrel and its talks of remodeling the restaurant interiors and refreshing the logo. Overall sales were not where the chain wanted them to be, and a revamp could potentially expand its customer base. However, due to heavy customer criticism, Cracker Barrel decided to halt any further rebranding. Isn&rsquo;t it a little funny how restaurants had suggestion boxes that were probably never opened, and now everyone on the internet has their opinions? We can&rsquo;t say it&rsquo;s not effective, though.</p><h2>Cracker Barrel Will Remain the Same After All</h2><p>Cracker Barrel was hoping to upgrade the interiors of its restaurants for a modernized look. On August 19, Cracker Barrel also presented a new logo. It was an updated version of the current logo with a sleeker font and without the recognizable &ldquo;old timer&rdquo; figure. However, longtime customers of the Southern-themed restaurant steadily voiced their opinions.</p><p>Due to the massive amount of <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2025/08/21/business/cracker-barrel-rebrand-logo.html" data-name="www.nytimes.com/2025/08/21/business/cracker-barrel-rebrand-logo.html" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">customer criticisms</a> and comments, Cracker Barrel decided to put a pause on its current remodel strategy and reverted back to the classic logo just a week later. The chain also <a href="https://www.crackerbarrel.com/allthemore" data-name="www.crackerbarrel.com/allthemore" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">issued a statement</a> about the pause.</p><p>While some were upset about the remodel itself, many others voiced concern about the food. If you know anything about Cracker Barrel, it&rsquo;s that it sure knows how to serve up a tasty <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/cracker-barrel-copycat-recipes/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/cracker-barrel-copycat-recipes/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Southern breakfast</a>. However, customers were hoping to see as much passion put into the food as was going into the remodel. Quite a few comments were about the quality of the food, saying the comfort dishes felt more like diner food as of late. If the chain&rsquo;s next focus is on the menu itself, I just hope the spiced apple butter doesn&rsquo;t change!</p><script async type="text/javascript" src="//tracking.skyword.com/tracker.js?contentId=281474980465043"></script><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/cracker-barrel-halts-plans-to-remodel/">The Fans Have Spoken: Cracker Barrel Is Halting Plans to Remodel</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/cracker-barrel-halts-plans-to-remodel/feed/
0
Chicken Gnocchi Pesto Soup
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/chicken-gnocchi-pesto-soup/
Nancy Mock
Wed, 10 Sep 2025 10:25:14 +0000

http://origin-www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/chicken-gnocchi-pesto-soup/
Chicken gnocchi pesto soup is rich and filling, yet takes less than 30 minutes to make. Get the crusty bread ready—you'll want it for dunking.
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>1 jar (15 ounces) roasted garlic Alfredo sauce</li><li>2 cups water</li><li>2 cups rotisserie chicken, roughly chopped</li><li>1 teaspoon Italian seasoning</li><li>1/4 teaspoon salt</li><li>1/4 teaspoon pepper</li><li>1 package (16 ounces) potato gnocchi</li><li>3 cups coarsely chopped fresh spinach</li><li>4 teaspoons prepared pesto</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>In a large saucepan, combine the first 6 ingredients; bring to a gentle boil, stirring occasionally. Stir in gnocchi and spinach; cook until gnocchi float, 3-8 minutes. Top each serving with 1 teaspoon pesto.</span></li></ol></div>

<div class="recipe-cooking-tips-title">
<h2>Potato gnocchi</h2>			</div>
Look for potato gnocchi in the pasta or frozen foods section.

We tried a <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/stanley-flask/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/stanley-flask/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Stanley flask</a> and loved it!</p><div class="ap-card-wrap"><div class="ap-card-image-wrapper"><div class="ap-card-img-container"><img decoding="async" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/A-New-Stanley-Halloween-Cup-Is-Coming_The_Everyday_Tumbler_16OZ_Via-Stanley1913.com_03.jpg?w=680" alt="The Everyday Tumbler 16oz" loading="lazy" data-recalc-dims="1" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="" title=" 4"></div></div><div class="ap-card-details"><div class="ap-card-details-header"><h3 class="ap-card-title">Stanley Halloween Everyday Tumbler</h3></div><div class="ap-card-details-footer"><p class="ap-card-button-wrap retailer-primary"><a class="ap-card-button" data-name="Shop at Stanley" data-module="affiliate no price button" data-position="" href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-halloween-everyday-tumbler-16-oz%3Fvariant%3D53973483553128" target="_blank" data-button-text="Shop at Stanley" data-retailer-name="Stanley" data-product-name="Stanley Halloween Everyday Tumbler" data-product-retailer="Stanley" data-product-type="skimlinks" rel="nofollow">Shop at Stanley</a></p></div></div></div><p>The <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-halloween-everyday-tumbler-16-oz%3Fvariant%3D53973483553128" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-halloween-everyday-tumbler-16-oz%3Fvariant%3D53973483553128" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Purple Night Shine Everyday tumbler</a> is shadowy, dreamy and a little eerie. The <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-halloween-reserve-wine-tumbler-11-oz%3Fvariant%3D53973483225448" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fproducts%2Fthe-halloween-reserve-wine-tumbler-11-oz%3Fvariant%3D53973483225448" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">11-ounce wine tumbler</a> keeps wine chilled, has a non-slip silicone base and stacks easily for storage.</p><h2>Where to Buy</h2><p>Heads up: <a href="https://go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fcollections%2Fhalloween" data-name="go.skimresources.com?id=131817X1598243&amp;xs=1&amp;url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.stanley1913.com%2Fcollections%2Fhalloween" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">The Stanley Halloween collection</a> comes with a slight price bump&mdash;about $5 more per item compared to the usual solid colors.</p><p>The full drop goes live September 16 at 9 a.m. PT / 12 p.m. ET, but if you&rsquo;re a <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/stanley-club/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/stanley-club/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Stanley Club member</a>, you get early access starting September 15 at the same time. Ina Garten Just Shared Her Easiest Appetizer Recipe Ever
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-easy-appetizer/
Hayley Schueneman
Wed, 10 Sep 2025 14:11:49 +0000
News
People in Food
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2181043
<p>It's as simple as can be, but is still guaranteed to impress.</p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-easy-appetizer/">Ina Garten Just Shared Her Easiest Appetizer Recipe Ever</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>There&rsquo;s something so soothing about watching Ina Garten prepare food. Whether it&rsquo;s on her TV show, <em>The Barefoot Contessa</em>, or simply on an Instagram Reel, she certainly gives me the boost of confidence I need.</p><p>Her recipes are consistently crowd-pleasers, and she pretty much has one for every occasion. Feeling blue? Grab a bowl of butternut squash soup, which happens to be <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-favorite-comfort-recipe/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-favorite-comfort-recipe/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">her favorite comfort food</a>. Need a dessert that&rsquo;ll wow at a potluck? Try Ina&rsquo;s <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-gartens-favorite-dessert/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-gartens-favorite-dessert/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">French apple tart</a> and wait for the compliments to roll in. Hosting can be stressful, but not if you channel Ina&rsquo;s sense of calm.</p><p>So while I don&rsquo;t live in the Hamptons, I like to channel the Barefoot Contessa&rsquo;s elevated nature whenever I have guests over. And Ina just dropped perhaps the easiest appetizer recipe that I have ever seen.</p><h2>What is Ina Garten&rsquo;s easy appetizer recipe?</h2><blockquote class="instagram-media" style="background: #FFF; line-height: 17px; text-decoration: none;" href="https://www.instagram.com/reel/DN3AafM4kTG/?utm_source=ig_embed&amp;utm_campaign=loading" data-name="www.instagram.com/reel/DN3AafM4kTG/?utm_source=ig_embed&amp;utm_campaign=loading" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">A post shared by Ina Garten (@inagarten)</a></p></div></blockquote><p><script async src="//www.instagram.com/embed.js"></script></p><p>While Ina is no stranger to <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/ina-garten-grilled-new-york-strips/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/ina-garten-grilled-new-york-strips/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">firing up the grill</a> for guests, she also has a few low-key recipes up her sleeve. Namely, a beautifully arranged Mediterranean mezze platter. It seems to combine two of Ina&rsquo;s favorite sayings into one beautiful dish: &ldquo;store bought is fine&rdquo; and &ldquo;how easy is that?&rdquo;</p><p>In a recent <a href="https://www.instagram.com/p/DN3AafM4kTG/?hl=en" data-name="www.instagram.com/p/DN3AafM4kTG/?hl=en" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow">Instagram</a> post, Ina says that she has friends coming over for cocktails, and that it&rsquo;s way too hot to cook. So, she shows viewers how she put together the platter&mdash;which requires zero cooking. &ldquo;I&rsquo;m going to make a Mediterranean mezze platter, completely with ingredients that I bought at the grocery store,&rdquo; she says in the video.</p><p>First, she lays some fig leaves on a wooden platter (a large cutting board is a great option, too) as a nice base for the spread. &ldquo;I take all of these ingredients, and I do something to them to make them special,&rdquo; she says. &ldquo;So it doesn&rsquo;t feel like you&rsquo;re cooking, but it also doesn&rsquo;t feel like it&rsquo;s from the store.&rdquo;</p><p>She slices a block of feta, then sprinkles it with herbes de Provence and drizzles it with olive oil. She also puts hummus into a bowl, then tops it with pine nuts and, you guessed it, olive oil. Additional ingredients include vine-ripened tomatoes, stuffed grape leaves and <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/baba-ganoush/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/baba-ganoush/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">baba ganoush</a> topped with pomegranate arils. Then, of course, plenty of pita bread for dipping!</p><p>As she builds the platter, the overall effect is one of beautiful simplicity. It&rsquo;s not going to be overwhelming to throw something like this together when you have guests visiting. I think it would pair nicely with <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/meghan-markle-wine-review-july-2025/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/meghan-markle-wine-review-july-2025/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">a refreshing glass of ros&eacute;</a>. How easy is that?</p><h2>Related:</h2><ul><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-pork-tenderloin/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-pork-tenderloin/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">Ina Garten&rsquo;s Unexpected Trick for Perfect Pork Tenderloin</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-engagement-chicken/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-engagement-chicken/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">I Made Ina Garten&rsquo;s &lsquo;Engagement Chicken,&rsquo; and People Love This Recipe for a Reason</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-cilantro/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-cilantro/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">This Is the One Ingredient Ina Garten Will Never Use in a Recipe</a></li></ul><p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/ina-garten-easy-appetizer/">Ina Garten Just Shared Her Easiest Appetizer Recipe Ever</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
I Tried the New Girl Scout Cookie, and I Already Want to Order More
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/new-girl-scout-cookie-2025/
https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/new-girl-scout-cookie-2025/#respond
Melany Love
Wed, 10 Sep 2025 00:14:26 +0000
New Products
News
Trends
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?p=2182294
<p>This rocky road-inspired treat is sure to be a hit this cookie season. </p>
<p>The post <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/new-girl-scout-cookie-2025/">I Tried the New Girl Scout Cookie, and I Already Want to Order More</a> appeared first on <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com">Taste of Home</a>.</p>
<p>At this point, Girl Scout cookies may as well be synonymous with the word delicious. Talk to anybody about Girl Scout cookies, and you <em>know</em> they have a favorite lined up. Mine happen to be Do-Si-Dos, also known as Peanut Butter Sandwiches. And while they&rsquo;re not everyone&rsquo;s idea of the <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-girl-scout-cookies/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/best-girl-scout-cookies/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">best Girl Scout cookies</a>, I still love them all the same. Trust me, they go <em>so</em> well dunked in a glass of milk.</p><p>Now, over the years, we&rsquo;ve seen Girl Scout cookies evolve. Some have been <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/discontinued-girl-scout-cookies/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/discontinued-girl-scout-cookies/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">discontinued</a> for a while, and others, like the <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/girl-scouts-discontinue-two-cookie-flavors-2025/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/girl-scouts-discontinue-two-cookie-flavors-2025/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">S&rsquo;mores and Toast-Yay! cookies</a> left us just this past year. Gone, but never forgotten. So what takes their place then? The Girl Scouts are always looking for their next new incredible cookie, and their latest flavor foray is already on the horizon. Luckily, I got an early taste. Buckle up&mdash;we&rsquo;re going on a very tasty trip.</p><h2>What is the new Girl Scout cookie?</h2><p><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-2182314" src="https://www.tasteofhome.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/I-Tried-the-New-Girl-Scout-Cookie_new-girl-scout-cookies-3_Melany-Love-for-TOH.jpg?fit=680%2C995" alt="" width="700" height="1024" data-recalc-dims="1" title="I Tried The New Girl Scout Cookie New Girl Scout Cookies 3 Melany Love For Toh" data-has-syndication-rights="1" data-portal-copyright="Melany Love for Taste of Home"></p><p>They&rsquo;re called Exploremores, and they are as delicious as they are intriguing. I&rsquo;m a big, big fan of a classic sandwich cookie. Like I said before, my favorite Girl Scout cookies of all time are Peanut Butter Sandwiches. Anyway, these new sandwich cookies are inspired by <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/collection/most-popular-ice-cream-flavor-in-every-decade/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/collection/most-popular-ice-cream-flavor-in-every-decade/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">rocky road ice cream</a> with all the fixins: chocolate, marshmallow and toasted almond. They were created to highlight the sense of exploration at the heart of every Girl Scout.</p><h2>How does the new Girl Scout cookie taste?</h2><p>Honestly, pretty close to the real thing. While rocky road was never too high on my list of favorite ice cream flavors, this cookie is making me do a double take. The two outside sandwich cookies are thick and riddled with rich chocolate flavor. The middle was a mix of marshmallow and almond creme. The chocolate cookies weren&rsquo;t overtly sweet or overwhelming to the other flavors. In fact, the cookies were quite almond-forward. Sometimes sweets can get a bit<em> too</em> sweet for my liking, but the Exploremores were a fantastic middle ground.</p><p>My one slight disappointment was the lack of marshmallow flavor. It was present under the layers of almond, but I wanted more! I&rsquo;m a massive marshmallow lover (I&rsquo;ll miss you, S&rsquo;mores cookies), and so anytime marshmallow is mentioned, I&rsquo;m usually all in. Maybe I&rsquo;ll just have to snack through a few more boxes to get my fill.</p><h2>When can I get the new Girl Scout cookie flavor?</h2><p>Exploremores will officially be part of the 2026 Girl Scout cookie lineup with boxes available both in-person at local booths and <a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/girl-scout-cookie-orders-online/" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/girl-scout-cookie-orders-online/" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links" rel="noopener noreferrer">online</a>. I know cookie season may seem far away, but don&rsquo;t worry. You&rsquo;ll be munchin&rsquo; on these delectable desserts in no time!</p><h2>Related:</h2><ul><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-tried-the-new-mcdonalds-gold-sauce-and-it-tastes-like-sweet-smoky-heaven/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/i-tried-the-new-mcdonalds-gold-sauce-and-it-tastes-like-sweet-smoky-heaven/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">I Tried the New McDonald&rsquo;s Gold Sauce and It Tastes Like Sweet, Smoky Heaven</a></li><li><a href="https://www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-genius-gourmet-sparkling-protein-drink-review/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-name="www.tasteofhome.com/article/costco-genius-gourmet-sparkling-protein-drink-review/?int_campaign=tmb_trend_recirc&amp;int_source=direct&amp;int_medium=tmb.com&amp;int_placement=single_card" data-module="content engagement" data-position="embedded links">A New Protein Drink Has Entered the Market, and You&rsquo;ll Never Guess What It Is</a></li><li><a Tyler Smith’s Pumpkin Spice BBQ Ribs
https://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/tyler-smith-pumpkin-spice-bbq-ribs/
Tyler Smith
Wed, 10 Sep 2025 00:13:29 +0000
Appliances
Creator
Gas Grill
Gear
Herbs & Spices
Ingredients
Meat & Poultry
Pork
Pork Ribs
Pumpkin Pie Spice
Pumpkins
Recipes
Vegetables
https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2182328
Pumpkin spice barbecue ribs are the perfect duo: It's game day meets pumpkin spice season! These ribs are a seasonal favorite at every tailgate for both barbecue and PSL fans. —Tyler Smith, Virginia Beach, Virginia
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>RIBS:</b></li><li>1 rack pork baby back ribs</li><li>6 to 8 tablespoons barbecue rub</li><li>4 to 6 tablespoons pumpkin pie spice</li><li class="ingredient-title"><b class='sIngredient'>PUMPKIN SPICE BARBEQUE SAUCE:</b></li><li>2 cups ketchup</li><li>1 cup canned pumpkin</li><li>1/2 cup cider vinegar</li><li>1/2 cup packed brown sugar</li><li>2 tablespoons Worcestershire sauce</li><li>2 tablespoons pumpkin pie spice</li><li>Optional: Toasted sesame seeds and sliced green onions</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">

<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>Prepare grill for indirect medium heat (about 325°). If necessary, remove thin membrane from ribs and discard. Slice into individual ribs.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a small bowl, combine barbecue rub and pumpkin pie spice; rub over ribs until well coated. Grill, covered, over indirect medium heat, 1-1/2 to 2 hours.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Meanwhile, in a saucepot, combine sauce ingredients until smooth. Cook over medium-high heat until mixture comes to a boil. Reduce heat to a simmer; cook until thickened, 10-15 minutes. Reserve 1/2 cup sauce for finishing.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Brush remaining sauce over ribs, covering well. Cook until tender and browned, about 1 hour longer.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Remove from heat. Brush with remaining sauce; let stand 15 minutes before serving. If desired, garnish with sesame seeds and sliced green onion.</span></li></ol></div>

Pumpkin spice cream rolls are the ultimate fall treat. Soft Hawaiian rolls are stuffed with a dreamy pumpkin spice cream filling and topped with silky pumpkin icing. They’re sweet, fluffy and just the right amount of cozy, making them perfect for crisp mornings. Pair them with a hot cup of coffee and you’ve got breakfast (or dessert!) that feels like a hug in every bite. —Alex Bala, Longmont, Colorado

https://www.tasteofhome.com/?post_type=recipe&p=2180347
Caramel apple focaccia bread is a gooey, sweet take on the viral no-knead focaccia trend that's been sweeping the internet.
<div class="recipe-ingredients">
<h2>Ingredients</h2>
<ul class="recipe-ingredients__list recipe-ingredients__collection splitColumns">
<li>2-1/2 cups bread flour</li><li>2-1/2 cups all-purpose flour</li><li>2 teaspoons salt</li><li>2 teaspoons quick-rise yeast</li><li>1 teaspoon sugar</li><li>2-1/4 cups warm water (110&deg; to 115&deg;)</li><li>2 tablespoons extra virgin olive oil plus more for greasing</li><li>3 tablespoons butter, divided</li><li>3 medium Granny Smith apples, peeled and diced</li><li>1 teaspoon ground cinnamon</li><li>1/3 cup apple butter</li><li>1 tablespoon turbinado (washed raw) sugar</li><li>1/2 cup caramel sauce</li><li>1/4 cup chopped unsalted peanuts, optional</li>		</ul>
<div class="recipe-ingredients__action-buttons">
<div id="text-ingredients-container">
<a href="sms:?&body=Caramel Apple Focaccia%20%0Ahttps://www.tasteofhome.com/recipes/caramel-apple-focaccia/%20%0A%20%0AINGREDIENTS%20%0A%20%0A2-1/2 cups bread flour%20%0A2-1/2 cups all-purpose flour%20%0A2 teaspoons salt%20%0A2 teaspoons quick-rise yeast%20%0A1 teaspoon sugar%20%0A2-1/4 cups warm water (110&deg; to 115&deg;)%20%0A2 tablespoons extra virgin olive oil plus more for greasing%20%0A3 tablespoons butter, divided%20%0A3 medium Granny Smith apples, peeled and diced%20%0A1 teaspoon ground cinnamon%20%0A1/3 cup apple butter%20%0A1 tablespoon turbinado (washed raw) sugar%20%0A1/2 cup caramel sauce%20%0A1/4 cup chopped unsalted peanuts, optional%20%0A" data-name="Text Ingredients" data-module="content engagement" data-position="mobile text recipe" target="blank" tabindex="0" aria-label="Link: Text Ingredients">

<g clip-path="url(#clip0_1070_10606)">
<path d="M13.0625 0.499023H5.1875C4.25586 0.499023 3.5 1.25488 3.5 2.18652V16.8115C3.5 17.7432 4.25586 18.499 5.1875 18.499H13.0625C13.9941 18.499 14.75 17.7432 14.75 16.8115V2.18652C14.75 1.25488 13.9941 0.499023 13.0625 0.499023ZM9.125 17.374C8.50273 17.374 8 16.8713 8 16.249C8 15.6268 8.50273 15.124 9.125 15.124C9.74727 15.124 10.25 15.6268 10.25 16.249C10.25 16.8713 9.74727 17.374 9.125 17.374ZM13.0625 13.5771C13.0625 13.8092 12.8727 13.999 12.6406 13.999H5.60938C5.37734 13.999 5.1875 13.8092 5.1875 13.5771V2.6084C5.1875 2.37637 5.37734 2.18652 5.60938 2.18652H12.6406C12.8727 2.18652 13.0625 2.37637 13.0625 2.6084V13.5771Z" fill="#005278"/>

<span>Text Ingredients</span>

<div class="recipe-ingredients-ad-wrapper">

<div class="recipe-directions">
<h2 class="recipe-directions__heading">
Directions	</h2>
<ol class="recipe-directions__list"><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>In the bowl of a stand mixer fitted with a dough hook, combine flours, salt, yeast, and sugar. Add&nbsp;water and olive oil; mix until a rough dough forms and no dry patches remain, 1-2 minutes. Cover; let rest for 5 minutes.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Perform a series of stretches and folds on the dough. Wet your hands; pinch a section of the dough along the outer edge. Stretch it up and fold it in towards the center of the dough. Rotate the bowl; repeat the process, working all the way around the circumference of the dough in the bowl, about 8-10 stretches total. Cover; let rest 3 minutes.&nbsp;Repeat the stretch and fold process 2 more times, for a total of 3 rounds, resting 3 minutes between the rounds.&nbsp;Drizzle dough lightly with additional olive oil; turn over to coat. Cover with plastic wrap; let rise in a warm place for 2 hours.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Coat a 13x9-in. baking sheet with olive oil; carefully turn the dough out onto the pan. Gently shape into a rough rectangle; let rest 10 minutes. Finish shaping the dough, extending it toward the edges and corners of the pan.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Drizzle lightly with olive oil to keep the dough moist; let rise, uncovered, until doubled in size, about 2 hours.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Towards the end of the rise, preheat oven to 450°F.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a small skillet, heat 1 tablespoon butter over medium heat. Add apples and cinnamon; cook until softened, 4-5 minutes. Remove from heat; set aside.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
In a small microwave-safe bowl, microwave remaining 2 tablespoons butter 30 seconds or until melted; stir in apple butter. Drop spoonfuls of apple butter mixture evenly over the risen dough; scatter apples on top.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
With well-oiled fingers, dimple the surface of the dough, pressing apples and apple butter into the dough to evenly distribute. Sprinkle top with turbinado sugar; bake 25-30 minutes or until deeply golden brown.</span></li><li class="recipe-directions__item"><span>
Let cool 5-7 minutes; drizzle generously with caramel sauce. Sprinkle with chopped peanuts, if desired. Slice; serve while warm.</span></li></ol></div>

<h2 class="recipe-nutrition-facts__heading">Nutrition Facts</h2>
<p>1 serving: 185 calories, 6g fat (2g saturated fat), 4mg cholesterol, 228mg sodium, 29g carbohydrate (7g sugars, 1g fiber), 4g protein.</p>
